poete tyme yt whiche wrote fayned gloryouſly many leſynge ¶ incipit regnum britannie nunc dicitur anglia ¶ may ye ſe englonde fyrſt began albyon albyon ¶ afore wyll ſpeke brute ſhall ſhewed londe englonde fyrſt named • byon cauſe ſo named noble londe sirrie noble kynge myghty man grete renome yt called diocleſyan well worthely hȳ gouerned ruled noble chyualry yt conquered londes hym ſo almooſt ye kynges worlde hȳ attendaūt befell thus yt diocleſian ſpouſed gētyll damoyſel yt wonder fayre yt vncles doughter labana ſhe loued hym reaſon wolde ſo yt gate xxxiij doughters yt whiche ye eldeſt called albyne theſe damoyſelles whan came vnto age came ſo fayre yt wonder whereof diocleſian anone let make ſomnynge cōmaunded lettres kynges yt helde hym ſholde come certayn daye lettres conteyned make feeſt royal whiche daye thyder came brought admyrats prince duke noble ch • ualry feeſt royally arayed lyued ioye myrth ynough yt wonder wyte befell thus ye dyocleſyan thought mary doughters amonge thoſe kynges yt ye ſolempnite ſo ſpake dyd albyne eldeſt doughter ſyſters rychely maryed xxxiij kynges yt lordes grete honour ſolempnite whan done euery kynge toke wyfe ladde theyr owne coūtre made quenes befell thus afterward yt dame albine became ſo ſtoute ſo ſterne ſhe tolde lytel pryce lorde hyȳ ſcorne deſpyte wold wyll ſhe wold haue owne wyll dyuers mater ſyſters euerychone bare ſo euyll agaynſt theyr lordes yt wonder wyte moche yt thought theyr huſbondes ſo hye parentage comē theyr fader thoſe kynges yt theyr lordes wold haue chaſtyſed fayre maner vpon al loue frendſhyp yt ſhold amende theyr euyll condicyons nought dyd theyr owne wyll thynge yt lyked power wherfore thoſe xxxiij kynges vpon tyme often tymes bette theyr wyues wende wold haueamended theyr tatches wyckednes ſuche condicions fayre ſpeche warnynge dyd ye worſe betynges eftſones moche worſe wherfore kyng yt wedded albyne wrote tatches condicyons wyfe albyne lettre ſent dyocleſyan fader whan kynges herde albynes lorde ſente lettre diocleſyan anone ſente lettres ſealed theyr ſeales condicyons tatches theyr wyues whan kynge diocleſyan ſawe herde ſo many complayntes doughters ſore aſhamed became wonderſſy angry wroth toward doughters thought myght amende ſo myſoyd anone ſent lettres xxxiij kynges yt ſholde come hym brynge wt theyr wyues euerychone certayn day wolde chaſtyſe theyr wyckednes yf myght ī ony maner wyſe ye kynges came ye tyme daye tho ſet bytwene hym kynges diocleſyan receyued wt moche honour made ſolem • e feeſt vnto vndernethe lordſhyp thyrde daye ſolempnite ye kynge diocleſyan ſent xxxiij doughters yt ſhold come ſpeke hym chambre whā come ſpake theyr wyckednes theyr cruelte angerly reproued blamed ſaid yf wolde chaſtyſed ſholde loſe loue euermore whan ye ladyes herde al became abaſſhed gretly aſhamed ſayd theyr fader yt wolde make amēdes ſo departed theyr faders chambre albyne ye eldeſt ſyſter ladde chambre tho made voyde al yt therin ſo yt pſone amonge ſhe ſyſters togyder thāſayd albyne fayre ſyſters well knowe yt kyng fader v hath reproued ſhamed deſpyſed bycauſe make v obedyent huſbondes certaynly yt ſhall neuer whyles ye ilyue ſyth come hyer kynges blode myn huſbonde whan ſhe thus ſaid ſyſters ſayd ye ſame ſayd albyne well wote fayre ſyſters yt huſbondes haue cōplayned vnto fader vpon v wherfore hath v thus foule reproued deſpyſed wherfore ſyſters coūſeyle yt night whan huſbōdes ben bedde wt one aſſent kytte theyr throtes may • pea better may vnder faders power thā ony el anone ye ladyes conſented graūted counſeyle whānyght comen lordes ladyes went bedde anone theyr lordes •• ept kytte theyr huſbōdes throtes ſo ſhewe whan diocleſian theyr fader herde thynge became wroth ryght furyouſly agaynſt doughters anone wole haue brent harons lordes • rrye counſeyled ſo ſuche ſtraytnes owne doughters ſhold boyde ye londe euermore ſo neuer ſholde come agayne ſo dyd diocleſyan yt theyr fader anone cōmaūded go ſhyppe delyuered • itayles halfe yere whan done ſyſters wente ſhyppe ſayled forth ye ſee betoke theyr frendes appolyn yt theyr god ſo longe ſayled ſee • yll laſt came arryued yle yt wyldernes whan dame •• yne come ye londe ſyſters •• byne went fyrſt forth ye ſhyppe ſayd ſyſters moche ye eldeſt ſyſter cōpany firſt londe haue take moche name alb • ne wyl • londe called albion •• owne name anone ſyſters graūted good wyll went ye ſhyppe ye ſyſters toke londe albion theyr ſyſter called went vp downe foūde neyther man ne woman ne chylde wylde beeſtes dyuers kyndes whan theyr • ttayles diſpruded ſayled fedde herbes fruytes ſeaſon yt yere ſo •• ued beſt myght yt toke fleſſhe dyuers beeſtes bera •• wonder fa •• e ſo deſyred mānes company mānes kynde fay • ed wexed wonder couragyous kynde ſo deſyred mannes company ony ſolace myrth whan deuyll yt per •• yued went dyuers coūtries toke body ye ayre lykyng nature ſh •• men came ye londe albion lay thoſe woman ſhad tho nature vpon conceyued brought forth gyaūtes whiche one called gogmagog another langerigan ſo named dyuers name maner came forth borne horryble gyaūtes albion dwelled caues hylles theyr wyll londe albion lyked vnto ye tyme brute arryued came totnes yt yle albion brute cōquered diſcōfyted ye gyaūtes aboue ſayd ¶ explicit prima par ¶ begȳneth brute goten ſlewe fyrſt moder fader conquered albyon named brytayne owne name called englonde name engyſt saxonye brute came brytayne aboute xviij yere hely knowen ye noble cite grete troy noble knyght man grete power called eneas whan ye cite troy loſt deſtroyed grece eneas meyny fledde then came lombardy tho lorde gouernour londe kyng hyght latyne another kynge ye hyght turocelyne ſtrongly warred vpon kynge latyne ye oftentymes dyd hym moche harme whan kynge latyne herde yt eneas come receyued hym moche honour hym helde moche herd hȳ wyſt well yt noble knight worthy body dedes eneas helped kynge latyne wa ••• ſhortly tell ſo well ſo worthely dyd ſlewe turocelyne dyſcomfyted hym people whan done kyng latyne gaue ye londe turocelynes noble man eneas • maryage lauyne doughter mooſt fayreſt creature ony man wyſt ſo lyued togyder ioye myrth dayes theyr lyues ¶ aſcanius ſone eneas wedded wyfe vpon gate ſone called siluine siluyne whan coude ſome reaſon man vnwytyng fader agaynſt wyll acqueynted hym wt damoyſel coſyn lauyne kynge latynes doughter ye quene eneas wyfe brought damoyſell chylde whan aſcanius fader wyſt anone let enquyre wyſeſt mayſters greteſt clerkes chylde damoyſell ſholde brynge forth anſwered ſayd ſhe ſholde brynge forth ſone ſhold kyll bothe fader moder ſo dyd moder dyed berynge hym whan chylde borne fader let call hym brute ye mayſters ſayd ſholde moche harme ſorowe many dyuerſe place ſholde come grete honour worſhyp kyng aſcanius dyed whan god wolde siluyne ſone receyued londe made hym wonder • ly well beloued among people ſo whā brute siluynes ſone xv yere olde went vpon daye fader playe ſolace brute ſhold haue ſhotte vnto hart arowe myſhapped glanced ſo brute ſlewe fader ¶ brute dryuen londe helde hym grece whan miſchaūce befallen ye people londe made grete ſorowe ſore dyſpleaſed bycauſe therof droue brute ye londe wolde ſuffre hym amonge whan ſawe might abyde went then grece foūde vij thouſande men ye kynrede troye comen grete blode ſtory telleth men woman child whiche holden thraldome bondage kyng pandras grece ye deth achylles betrayed ſlayne troy brute wōders fayre man ſtronge huge age gladde chere ſemblaūt alſo worthy body well beloued amōge people kyng pandras herde ſpeke goodnes condicyons anone made hym dwell hym brute became wonder preuy moche beloued ye kynge dwelled longe tyme kynge ye laſt troy brute ſpake togyder kynrede lygnage acqueyntaūce complayned vnto brute theyr ſorowe theyr bondage many ſhames ye kynge pandras done brute ſayd vpon tyme ye lord lignage ſtronge man myghty ye capytayne gouernour wyll become men fulfyll al cōmaū dementes brynge v wret chednes bondage wyll fyght wt kyng trouth grace ye grete god ſhall ouercome hym ſhall make kynge londe homage ſhall holde euermore brute tho grete pyte theyr bondage yt brought pryuely went fro ye kynges courte tho troy went put woodes moūtaynes helde ſente vnto kynge pandras ſholde gyue lycence departe ſafely lōde kyngdom wolde longer dwell bondage whan kyng pandras herde ſore vexed anoyed tho ſware wolde • e euerychone ordeyned grete power went towardes fyght brute men manly defended fyerſly fought ſlewe kynges men none eſcaped toke ye kynge put hym pryſon ordeyned coūſeyle amonge ſelfe myght wt kynge ſome ſayd ſholde put deth ſome ſayd ſholde exyled londe ſome ſayd yt ſholde brent ſpake wyſe knyght yt called mempris ſayd brute troy yf kyng pandras wolde yelde hym haue lyfe coūſeyle yt gyue vnto brute duke ſouerayn doughter ge •• og •• wyfe maryage hondred ſhyppes well arayed treaſour golde ſyluer corne wyne moche nede one thynge go londe ordeyne v lōde el none kynrede yt come v ſhall neuer haue pea londe amonge grece haue •• ayne ſo many theyr knyghtes frendes euermore warre dyſcord ſhall amonge v brute tho folke conſented gladly ye coūſeyle thȳge tolde kyng pandras haue lyfe graūted moche demaunded anone gaue vnto brute fayre lady gennogen doughter wyfe hondred ſhyppes moche 〈◊〉 vytayles afore ordeyned thā brute toke wyfe men forſoke londe grete went ſee wynde weder theyr wyll came thyrde daye yle called logres brute anone ſent men londe eſpye ye maner ye coūtrce founde olde cite waſted forlet ſo neyther man womā therin dwellynge myddle cyte foūde olde temple fayre lady called diane goddeſſe came agayne vnto brute tolde hym ſeen foūde coūſeyled hym go ſacrifyce vnto dame diane ſhe wont gyue anſwere thynge mē aſked namely vnto honour ſacryfyce brute wente vnto yt ymage ſayd diane noble goddeſſe thynge haſt thy myght wyndes water woodes feldes thynges ye worlde maner beeſtes ben therin vnto make prayer ye coūſeyle tell plāce ſhall haue cōuenyent place dwell folke ſhall make honour fayre temple noble wherin ye ſhall alwaye honoured whan done prayer diane anſwered maner brute ſayd ſhe go euen forth thy way ouet ſee fraūce towarde weſt ye ſhal fynde yle called albion yle becompaſſed ſee man may come therin ſhyppes londe wont dwell gyauntes ſo wyldernes londe deſtenyed ordeyned people ¶ coryn became brute man kynge goffar diſcomfyted whan brute anſwere diane goddeſſe anone let wȳde vp ancres ſayled hye ſee whā men ſayled xx dayes foūde fall beſyde cooſt ſee men kynrede troy theyr ſouerayne mayſter called coryn whan brute wyſt whens toke wt moche ioye ſhyppes ſo ladde forth hym coryn became brute man hȳ dyd homage ſo lōge ſayled forth ſee tyll came gaſcoyne anone arryued ye hauen lyegers dwelled viij dayes reſt amende theyr ſayles nede ty dynges ſoone came kyng goffar lord londe moche people ſtraunge londe arryued londe hauen lyegers wherfore ſore angred anoyed came arriued londe without lycence leue anone ordeyned hym grete power dryue brute deſtroye hym people ſo ye kynge goffar dyſcomfyted people hymſelfe fledde fraunce haue helpe ſocour yt tyme regned fraunce xij kynges xj aſſembled grete power belpe goffar fyght agaynſt brute goffar dwelled wt kynges fraūce halfe yere meane tyme goffar fraūce brute company deſtroyed londe gaſcoyne let take treaſour kynge goffar made brought ſhyppes ¶ brute foūde londe fayre place conueny ent let make fayre caſtell ſtronge whan done kynge goffar came fraunce xj kynges hym brought wt hym xx men fyght brute company brute vij iij c men neuer theles whan ye two hooſtes mette togyder brute folke helpe hym ſelfe turyn coſyn coryn y• well manly defended ſo y• within whyle ſlayne y• frenſhmen moo two anone tho y• alyue fledde away batayle turin brute coſyn ſlayne brute let bury hym worthely whan ſpace ye caſtell yt made tho let call yt ſame caſtell tour bycauſe name turin yt buryed yet vnto daye noble cite yt called tour whan kyng goffar wyſt yt turyn deed came agayne wt men gaue ſtronge batayle brute brute men ſo wery fightȳge yt might longer endure went caſtel wt men made y• gate faſt ſaue toke coūſeyle amōge ſholde brute coryn gaue coūſeyle ordeyned pryuely y• coryn ſhold go buſſhe hym wode tyll y• morowe ſo yt mornynge whan brute ſholde fyght wt enemyes coryn ſhold come wt folke ye one ſyde ſlee ye harme yt myght morowe dawnynge y• daye brute wente caſtel fought fyerſly wt enemyes manly defended within lytell tyme brūte men ſlewe viij hondred kynge goffer men came corin wt buſſhemēt company ſmote groūde thoſe y• wolde ſtande abyde ſo ye kynge goffar company diſcomfyted faſt began flec brute coryn theyr company fyerſly purſued ſlewe moo fleynge dyd y• batayle maner brute y• victory neuertheles brute made moche ſorow coſyn turyn ſlayne alſo loſt men ſaye vij hondred xv whiche nobly buryed ſame caſtell tour buryed turyn coſyn ¶ brute arryued totnes yle called albyon wraſtlyng bytwene coryn gogmagog whā done brute wold longer dwell fyght loſe men kyng goffer people myght euery day encreaſe moo moo brute men leſſed therfore toke men wente vnto ſee wynde weder theyr wyll fyfth daye arryued hauen cornes came realme yt called albyon founde neyther man woman ſaue grete gyauntes dwelled mountaynes cauernes brute ſawe londe fayre ly kynge good alſo hym people diane ye goddeſſe behyght hym therof brute wonder gladde let aſſemble vpon daye folke make ſolempne ſacrifyce grete feeſt ye honour reuerēce diane goddeſſe whiche coūſeyled hȳ fyrſt come londe whā done theyr ſolē pnite ſate theyr meet vpon daye came vpon xxx gyauntes ſlewe xxx brute men brute mē anone ſtert vp fought gyauntes ſlewe euerychone ſaue one yt called gogmagog mayſter y• gyaūtes ſtrōger hyer ony brute kepte hym wraſtle corin man greter hyer • ny brute men gyrdelſtede vpwarde gogmagog corin vndertoke wraſtle ſo togyder went wraſtled lōge tyme laſt gogmagog helde coryn ſo faſt yt brake two rybbes ſyde wherfore coryn ſore angry toke gogmagog bytwene armes caſt hym downe vpon roche ſoo gogmagog brake peces ſo dyed euyll deth therfore place called yet vnto day ſaute gogmagog thā brute gaue coūtree vnto corin corin called name cornewayle men ben called cornewayles ſo ſholde men countree called euermore countree dwelled corin men made townes houſes euhabyted londe theyr owne wyll ¶ brute buylded london called londe brytayn scotlonde albanye wale cambar ¶ london brute men wente forth ſawe aboute dyuerſe place yt myght fynde good place couenable myght buylde make cyte hym folke ſo laſt came fayre ryuer whiche called temmes brute began buylde fayre cyte called newe troye remembraunce grete troye whiche place theyr lygnage comen brute let fell downe wodes let ere ſowe londes let mawe medowes ye ſuſtenaūce hȳ people thā departed ye londe ſo yt eche parte place dwell thā brute let call londe brytayne name folke brytons brute gotē wyfe gennogen iij ſones yt worthy dedes ye firſt called lotryn ye ſeconde albanak thyrde cambar brute bare crowne cite newe troy xx yere y• tyme ye cyte made made lawes yt briton holde brute wonderſly well ioued amonge people brute ſones alſo loued wonderſly well togyder whan brute ſought londe length brede founde londe yt ioyned brytayne north londe brute gaue albanak ſone let call albanye name yt called scotlonde brute foūde countree warde weſt gaue cambar ſone let call cambar name called wale whan brute regned xx yere dyed cite newe troye ¶ lotryn brute ſone entred moche honour gouerned londe well worthely brute regned lotryn ſone ye ſeconde kynge brytayn began regne ſeconde yere samuel lotryn crowned kyng wt grete ſolempnite brytayne whā crowned kyng albanak cambar bretherne departed theyr owne coū tree lyued moche honour worſhyp lotryn regned well wyſely moche beloued people befell ſo yt albanak dwelled owne londe wt moche honour worſhip came kyng hum bar hunlonde grete power •• ryued albanye wold haue cōque ••• londe began warre vpon albanak ſlowe hȳ batayle whan albanak deed people ye lōde fledde vnto lotryn tolde bycauſe kynge brytayne yt broder ſlayne prayed hym helpe ſocour auenge broders deth lotryn thā anone let aſſemble brytons kent douer vnto derewent norfolke suffolke keft fen lyndeſſey whan aſſembled ſped faſt towarde theyr enemyes gyue batayle lotryn ſente cambar broder yt ſholde come vnto hym ye power myght make helpe hym auenge broders deth ſo dyd good wyll whan came togider toke theyr waye pryuely go ſeke kynge humbar myght fynde hym ſo befell kynge humbar beſyde water grete ryuer folke dyſporte hym came lotryn cambar broder theyr folke ſodeynly ony theyr enemyes wyſt whan humbar ſawe come ſore adrad moche men wyſt 〈◊〉 afore alſo vnarmed anone humbar drede 〈◊〉 water drowned hymſelfe ſo dyed men flayne ſo moche eſcaped one awaye lyue therfore water called humbar euermore ſhall longe worlde ſtandeth bycauſe kynge humbar drowned therin locryn went ſhyppes toke golde ſyluer moche founde vnto himſelfe pylfre gaue vnto folke hooſt founde one ſhyppes fayre damoyfell whiche kynge humbars doughter ſhe called eſtrylde whan kynge lotryn ſawe toke hym bycauſe grete beaute fayrnes ſawe ouertaken loue wolde haue wedded theſe tydynges came corin anone thought auenge hym lotryn moche lotryn promiſed hym wedde guentolyn doughter corin haſte toke waye newe troy vnto hym ſayd thus lotryn certes ye rewarde full euyll ye paynes haue fader brute wher fore ſyth ſo wyll auenge yt drewe ſwerde wolde haue ſlayne lotryn ye kyng damoyſel went bytwene made accorded maner lotryn ſholde take guentolyn corins doughter wyfe ſo lotryn dyd neuertheles maryed wente pryuely eſtrylde gate doughter called abram befell ſo yt anone corin dyed whan deed lotryn forſoke guentolyn wyfe made themſelfe l yere wtout kyng befell afterwarde y• grete prynce came fro rome londe y• called seuerye warre ſaue ye ryght rome neuertheles dwelled halfe yere londe yt brytons ſlewe hym whan ye romayns hym water wherfore y• water called euermore walbroke regned aſclepades pea tyll one erles yt called coyl made fayre towne agaynſt ye kynges wyll let call y• towne colcheſtre name wherfore kynge wroth thought deſtroye hym began warre vpon hȳ brought grete power men gaue ye erle batayle erle defended hym fyerſly power ſlewe ye kynge hymſelfe batayle thā coyll crowned made kynge londe coyll regned nobly well beloued ye brytons whan y• romayns herde y• aſclepades ſlayne wonder glad ſent grete prȳce y• romayns called conſtance came kynge coyll chalenge y• trybute rome graūted hym full gladly accorded y• kyng coyll gaue hym doughter eleyne wyfe y• bothe fayre wyſe well lettred dwelled togyder loue ſoone kyng coyll dyed xiij yere regne lyeth colcheſtre ¶ conſtance romayn ſpouſed eleyne eleyne ſone yt called cōſtantyne kyng bare true fayth truly dyd rome lyfe whā regned xv yere dyed lyeth yorke ¶ conſtantyne kynge conſtances ſone ſone ſaynt eleyne gouerned ruled londe emperour rome kynge conſtance deth regned conſtantyne ſone ſone ſaynt eleyne foūde y• holy croſſe holy londe cōſtantyne became emperour rome befell tyme emperour rome yt ſaraſyn tyraūt yt called maxence whiche put deth al y• byleued god deſtroyed holy chirche power ſlewe chryſtē men myght fynde amōge let martyr ſaynt katheryne many chriſten people yt drede deth fled came londe kyng conſtantyne tolde hym y• ſorowe maxence dyd chryſtē folke wherfore cōſtantyn pite made grete ſorow aſſembled grete hoſt grete power went ouer vnto rome toke cyte ſlewe y• therin myſ byleue made emperour good man gouerned hym ſo well y• londes hȳ attendaūt vnder gouernaūce ¶ deuyll tyraūt 〈…〉 y• tyme londe grece herde theſe tydȳges ſodeynly became wood dyed ſodeynly ¶ whan conſtantyne went londe rome toke hȳ moder eleyne grete prudence thre grete lordes y• 〈◊〉 mooſt loued one called howell y• taberne ye thyrde mo 〈…〉 toke londe kepe ye erle cornewayle called octauian anone octauian wyſt lorde dwelled rome incontynent ceſed londe handes therwith dyd wyll amōge 〈◊〉 lowe helde hym kyng whan theſe tydynges came cōſtantyne emperour wonder wroth towarde erle octauyan ſent taberne xij men agaynſt hym arryued porteſmouth whan octauian wyſt let aſſembled grete power brytons dyſcomfyted hym taberne fledde scotlonde ordeyned grete power came agayne londe another tyme gyue batayle octauyan whan octauyan vnderſtode aſſembled grete power came towarde taberne faſt myght ſo thoſe two hooſtes mette togyder staneſmore ſtrongly ſmote togyder octauyan dyſcōfyted fledde then vnto norway taberne ſeaſed ye londe handes bothe townes caſtelles octauyan came agayne fro norway grete power droue al ye romayns made kyng lond ¶ maximian emperours coſyn rome ſpouſed octauyans doughter made kynge londe octauian gouerned ye londe well nobly none heyre ſaue doughter yōge chylde loued moche lyf moche waxed ſeke poynt deth might longer regne wolde haue made one neuewes kyng noble knyght ſtronge man yt called conan meriedok ſhold haue kepte kynges doughter haue maryed whan tyme ben lordes ye londe wolde ſuffre gaue coūſeyle maryed ſome hygh man grete honour thā might ſhe haue al luſt coūſeyle lord cōſtātyne ye emperour coūſeyle accorded choſe cador cornewayle go ye emperour meſſage toke ye waye went rome tolde emperour theſe tydynges well wyſely ye emperour ſent londe hym owne coſyn vncles ſone noble knyght ſtronge yt called maximyan ſpouſed octauyans doughter crowned kyng londe ¶ maximian emperours coſyn cōquered ye londe amorican gaue conan meriedok kyng maximian became ſo ryall yt thought conquere ye londe amorican ye grete rycheſſe yt herde tell y• londe ſo yt ne left man worthynes knyght ne ſquyer ne none mā yt ne toke wt ye grete domage ye lōde lefte home man kepe ye londe wt hym xxx knyghtes good mennes bodyes went ouer londe amorican ſlewe kyng called imball conquered londe whan ſo done called conan ſayd moche kyng octauyan wolde haue made kyng brytayn ye let dyſtroubled y• ye kyng gyue lōde amorican make kyng therof moche ye bryton wyl lōde haue ſame name called amorican ſhall called lytell brytayne londe fro whens comen ſhall called fro hen forth grete brytayne ſo ſhall men knowe one brytayne fro thā conan meriedok thanked hȳ curteyſly ſo made kynge lytell brytayn whan done maximyan went then vnto rome made emperour conſtantyne conan meriedok dwelled lytell britayn moche honour let ordeyne two plowman londe ere londe harowe ſowe feffed rychely yt moche kynge conan none knyghtes ne none people wolde take wyues nacyon fraūce ſent grete brytayne ye erle cornewayle men called dio nothe ſholde choſe lōde xj maydens ſaye viij meane people iij ye greteſt lordes ſholde ſpouſe whā dionothe vnderſtode made cōmaūdement londe brytayn many nombre came aſſembled togyder maydēs man durſt withſtande cōmaūdemēt bycauſe protectour whan theſe maydens aſſembled let come hym london let ordeyne ſhyppes haſtely wt therto belonged toke doughter called vrſula ye fayreſt creature y• ony man wyſt wolde haue ſent kyng conan yt ſhold haue ſpouſed made quene ye londe ſhe made pryuely god vowe chaſtite yt fader wyſt ne none man lyuynge ¶ vrſula xj maydens company wente towarde lytell brytayne martyred coleyne vrſula thoſe vnto company xj maydens ſhe lady mayſtreſſe toke ſhyppynge one tyme water called tamyſe cōmaū ded kyn frendes almyghty god ſayled toward lytell brytayn whan comen ye hygh ſee ſtronge tēpeſt aroſe goddes wyll vrſula ſhyppes cōpany dryuē hunlōde tempeſt arryued y• hauen cite coleyne kynge londe called gowan y• cite whan wyſt tydynges ſo many fayre maydens arryued toke elga broder houſholde hym went ſhyppes ſe fayre company whan ſawe ſo fayre cōpany wold haue ouer • ayen haue taken fro theyr virgy 〈…〉 te vrſula good virgyn counſeyled prayed warned taught felawes ſhol •• defend theyr myght rather ſuffre deth ſuffre theyr bodyes defouled virgyns became ſo ſtedfaſt god defended grace none power ſhame wherfore kynge gowan ſort anoyed wrathe ſlewe euerychone anone ryght ſo thoſe virgyns martyred • god lye coleyn ¶ kynge gowan came deſtroye londe man grete power called gracian defended londe whan done kynge gowan whiche ſaraſyn called hym broder elga ſayd hym ſholde go conquere londe thoſe fayre maydens borne thā ordeyned grete power pehites denmarke orkeney norway came londe brent townes ſlewe folke caſt chirches houſes religyon robbed londe length brede put deth thoſe wolde forſake ye ryght byleue chryſtēdom moche ſouerayne yt myght helpe kyng maximian taken wt hym ye worthy men therin ſo man ſo hardy name god yf dyd put ſtraūge deth byſſhop london yt tho whiche called goſſelyn ſcaped went then rome ſeke ſocour helpe deſtroye ſaraſyns deſtroyed londe romayns ſayd yt ben ſo often anoyed theyr ſendyng folke britayne helpe briton wold ſo ſo byſſhop goſſelyn went then without ony ſocour helpe went ye kyng lytell brytayne yt called aldroie ye thyrde kyng gowan meriedok ſayd vortimer poyſoned engiſt went kent ſeaſed ye londe hādes hym men became within lytel whyle ſo grete power ſo moche people men wyſt litel tyme whiche ye kȳges men whiche engyſtes wherfore brytons hym drede ſayd amonge yf ne toke coūſeyle bytwene londe ſhold deſtroyed engiſt people vortiger ye kyng begotē fyrſt wyfe thre ſones ye fyrſt called vortimer ſeconde catagren ye thyrde paſſent brytōs without ende ¶ ye kyng let ſeke merlin wale ſpeke hym whan kyng herde cō maūded meſſengers anone go wale ſeke chylde yf myght fynde hym ſholde brynge hym forth vnto hym recorde wytnes thynge taken lettres ne deſtroubled man ne lette ye meſſengers went then ſpedde ſo faſt came town called karmardyne paſſed forth theyr waye foūde two chyldren xxiiij yere age chydynge togyder haſty wordes one moder ¶ meſſengers kynge vortiger whan herde ſtryfe bytwene ye two gromes aſked yt ſtode beſyde whens merlyn borne alſo nouryſſhed hym tolde yt grete gentylwoman karmardyne called adhan moder none knewe fader whan kynges meſſengers herd theſe tydȳges went anone hym wardeyne ye towne tolde hym ye kynges wyll ſhewed hym lettre wherfore comen thyder merlyn moder anone fetched wardeyn ye towne cōmaūded thē ſholde go ye kynge meſſengers merlyn moder went then came vnto ye kyng receyued wt moche honour ye kyng aſked lady yf yt chylde ſone hym begate lady anſwered full tenderly wepynge ſayd ſhe neuer company man worldly ſyr ſayd ſhe whan yonge mayden faders chambre wt grete lignage cōpany oftē tymes went ſporte left alone chambre wolde go forth brēnynge ye ſonne came tyme fayre bacheler entred ī chambre alone came wyſt neuer ne yet knowe ye dores faſt barred wt dyd game loue myght power defende hȳ oftē came ye fore ſayd maner ſo yt begate chylde neuer myght wyte ¶ anſwere merlyn vpon kynges caſtell wolde ſtande whan merlyn herde moder ſayd ſpake kynge maner ¶ syr begoten aſke ye falleth none knowe tell ye cauſe wherfore brought wherfore ye haue ſent certes quod kynge wyſe coūſeylers haue done vnderſtande ye morter werke haue begon behoueth tēpred blode foūdament ſhall fayle euermore syr ſaid merlin wyll ye ſlee blode tempre morter ye quod kynge elles ſhall neuer caſtell ſtāde coūſeylers tell anſwered merlyn kyng syr ſaid let come thoſe wyſe coūſeylers wyll preue ſaye well ne truly whan wyſe men comen merlyn aſked yf blode cauſe make ye werke ſtande endure thoſe wyſe men abaſſhed coude anſwere ſayd merlyn ye kyng syr ſhall tell cauſe wherfore werke thus falleth may ſtande vnder moūtayn ye buylde toure grete pond water bottom ye ponde vnder water two dragon one whyte reed fyght togyder agaynſt werke ye depe myne tyll men come pond men take away ye water ye ſhal ſe dragon haue tolde yt fight togyder agaynſt werke cauſe wherfore foūdament vter broder arryued totnes grete hoſt anone brytons aſſembled went receyue aurilambros vter grete noblenes brought london crowned aurilambros made hym kyng dyd vnto hym homage anone aſked vortiger myght foūde kynge wolde auenged broders deth wolde warre vpon ye paynyms tolde hym vortiger wale ſo ladde hym thyder warde vortiger wyſt well thoſe bretherne came conquere hym fledde then caſtell called gerneth ſtode vpon hye moūtayne helde hym aurilambros vter broder theyr folke beſyeged caſtell full longe tyme caſtell ſtronge well arayed laſt keſt wylde fyre brente houſes men theyr araye moche within caſtell vortiger brent amonge ſo dyed moche ſorowe ¶ engiſt kent regned herde theſe tydynges anone fledde wolde haue gone scotlonde haue ſocoure aurilambros folke mette hym north countree gaue hym batayle engiſt men defended whyles yt myght folke dyſcomfited ſlayne otta ſone fledde vnto yorke aurilambros folowed hym egerly otta ſtode hym lytell whyle afterwarde put hym mercy aurilabros receyued hym hym men gaue countree galeway scotlonde dwelled kynge aurilambros went londe put awaye name engyſt londe engyſt name called let call agayne grete brytayne let make agayn chirches houſes paynyms wherof knyght called ambry ſomtyme foūder hous therfore hyll called mount ambryan called ambeſbury ſhall ſo euermore ¶ aurilambros dyd redreſſe londe grete brytayne whiche deſtroyed saxon ſuche gyauntes ſet grete good themſelfe euery tyme yt woūded ony maner hurt waſſhed ye ſtones hote water thā waſſhed therwith anone hole ¶ brytons went ſeke grete ſtones irlonde whā theſe britōs herd thȳge went ſwore amonge wolde goo ſeke thoſe ſtones toke vter kȳges broder theyr chefe capitayn v mē merlin coūſeyled go vnto irlonde ſo dyd whan kynge irlonde yt called guillomer herde tell ye ſtraūgers arriued londe aſſembled grete power fought agaynſt folke diſcōfyted brytons wente tyll came moūt kylian clymmed vp vnto moūt whan ſawe ſtones maner ſtode grete meruayle ſayd bytwene themſelfe man ſholde remeue ſtrength ne engyne ſo grete ſo lōge merlin thrugh crafte remeued brought theyr ſhyppes came agayn londe merlin ſet ye ſtones kyng wolde haue ſet ſame maner ſtode irlonde whan ye kynge ſawe yt made thāked merlin ryche ly hym rewarded wyll let call ye place stonehenge euermore ¶ paſſent yt vortigers ſone kyng guillomer came londe traytour called cappa empoyſoned ye kyng aurilambros men ſhall vnderſtāde ye paſſent yt vortigers ſone liued ſame tyme came lond wt grete power arryued ye north coū tre wold auēged faders deth vortiger ſtrongly truſted vpon ye com pany brought wt hym londe germany conquered ye north coūtre vnto yorke whā kyng aurilambros herde aſſem bled grete power briton went fyght paſſent diſcomfyted paſſent al people paſſent eſcaped then ſome men fledde then irlōde came kyng guillomer prayed hym helpe ſocour kynge graūted hym wt good wyll ſayd yt wold helpe hym vpon couenaunt ſelfe muſt go power brytayne wold auenge vpon brytons huge lyghtes bryght ony fyre brennynge one beme toward fraūce ſtreyght ouer ſee thyderwarde ye beme came vij bemes full clere longe ye lyght fyre ſterre ſeen many man none wyſt betokened vter kyng ¶ kyng vter begate igreyne erles wyfe cornewayle arthur kynge merlyn crafte yt coude chaunged y• kynges fygure lykenes erle vlfin garloys chamberleyn ye fygure iordan y• erles chamberleyn ſo y• eche hym ioyouſly wt moche honour thoſe two hoſtes mette aſſembled toke theyr waye nichol cheldrik beſyeged taken came vpon cheldrik people wiſt aſſayled thē egerly kyng cheldrik men defended manly theyr power kyng arthur men ſlewe ſo many ſaxons y• neuer ſeen ſuch ſlaughter cheldrik men yt left alyue fledde away kyng arthur purſued droue thē wode yt myght ferder paſſe cheldrik mē ſawe well brought grete diſeaſe yelded kyng arthur maner wiſe ſhold take theyr horſes harneys yt wold onely go fote theyr ſhyppes ſo wold go home theyr lōde neuer come agayn londe vpon aſſuraūce thynge gaue hym good hoſt age arthur counſeyle men graunted thynge receyued hoſtages thervpon ye ſaxons went theyr ſhyppes whan hye ſee wynde chaūged ye deuyll wold turned theyr nauy came agayne londe arryued cotnes went ye body gawayn coſyn ye body augniſſel let yt one borne ſcotlond pouer buried king arthur toke waye deſtroye mordred fled then corne wayle quene gueneuer yt kynge arthur wyfe yt thā ſoiourned yorke herde mordred fled then yt myght endure agaynſt kyng arthur ſhe ſore aferde grete doubte wyſt beſt ſhe wyſt well yt lorde kynge arthur wolde neuer haue mercy grete ſhame yt ſhe done hȳ toke waye baron concluded go ſeke dane fyght ſo rode y• nyght morowe aboute pryme came abyngdon y• dane thankkyng alured baron aſſem bled egerly aſſayled dane gaue ſtronge batayle dane long tyme put man wyſt whether parte loſt mooſt folke thus befell god wolde yt kyng alured victory wt moche honour dane ſo dryuen ne wyſt whether turne xv dayes kyng purſued wyll glad fayne ſpeke pea toke hym good hoſtage frenſſhmen none myght breke ye ordynaunce thoſe choſers empyre pope otto made ony blame ſaxons eſchewe petylles come theyr name ben wryten latyn lerned men theſe verſes magun • inenſis treuerenſis colonienſis quilibet imperij fit cancellarius horum et palatinus dapifer dux portitor enſis marchio prepoſitus camere pincerna bohemus hij ſtatuunt dominū cūctis per ſecula ſummū palati • ꝰ eſt come reni marchio eſt brandeburgenſis dux saxonū et rex bohemorū verū vt quidam dicunt occaſyon egle hath loſt many fether ende ſhall made naked ¶ otto ye thyrde emperour xviij yere man worthy man dayes empyre wyſdome fader faythfull man chirche many batayles ꝓſpered bycauſe deuoute almyghty god ſayntes gaue myghty worſhyppyng vnto relykes ſayntes oftentymes viſyted holy place man crowned gregory coſyn laſt deceſſed rome ¶ anno domini iiij nota silueſter ſecond pope gregory iiij yere made pope helpe deuyll whome dyd homage ſholde gyue hym thynge deſyred called gylbert enemy gate hym grace ye kynge fraūce made hym byſſhop remenſis anone depoſed gate grace emperour made byſſhop rauennie pope ende anone ſo haue put theyr hope fals deuyls yet men truſt ſaluacyon certayne demonſtracions ſepulture ye grete penaūce yt dyd laſt ende made handes legges cut diſmēbred body made caſt dore foules body drawen wt wylde beeſtes buryed ſo euer reſted hoūde ſtode ſtyll ſaynt iohn de latrans buryed ſigne ſaluacyon ¶ iohānes xviij pope v monethes ¶ iohannes xix pope hym fyue yere theſe two dyd lytel thȳges ¶ henricus ye fyrſt emperour almayn xx yere henry duke barry accordyng choſen blyſſed fame good name whiche redde many theſe duke barry holy men onely abſteynynge fleſſhly deſyres alſo vertuous lyuyng henry ſyſter holy whome gaue wyfe vnto kynge hungary ſhe brought hungary vnto right byleue chryſten fayth wyues name san •• ro •• ogundis whome lyued virgyn dayes lyfe made many batayle well ytaly almayn agayuſt rebelled proſpered ryght wyſly euermore laſt blyſſed ende deceſſed lyf ſaynt laurence wyfe put enſamples bycauſe theyr holy vertuous lyuynge ¶ benedictꝰ pope iohn xi yere man grete ſtryfe dayes put put benedictus deed ſeen holy byſſhop wretched fygure grete payne fygure ſayd truſted thynge mercy god thynge profyted hym done hym goten extorcyon vniuſtly thā byſſhop lefte byſſhopryche drede ſight went monaſtery lyued vertuouſly dayes ¶ iohānes ye xx pope hym xi yere lytell profyted ¶ kyng knoght dane deth eldred knoght daue begā regne edmund irenſyde yt king eldredes ſone fyrſt wyfe ordeyned grete power men began warre kynge knoght ſo dyd many tymes ofte warre ſo ſtrōge harde ye wonder wyte quene emme yt dwelled weſtmynſter grete drede two ſones alured edward leſt ſholde deſtroyed ye warre wherfore ſhe ſente ouer ſee normandy duke richard theyr vncle dwelled ſafete pea lōge tyme ¶ edmund irenſyde knoght dane warred fyerſly togyder ye laſt accorded maner ſholde departe realme bytwene ſo dyd loued togyder lyke two bretherne ¶ kyng edmund irenſyde ſlayne treaſon traytour yt called edryth stratton regned kyng edmūd irenſyde knoght ye dane thus befel afterward yt ye ſame yere accorded ſo moche loued togyder wherfore fals traytour enuy loue bytwene whoſe name edrith ſtra • • grete lorde yt edmunde irenſydes man hym helde londe neuertheleſſe thought betraye lorde make knoght kyng londe entent rychely auaūced hym well beloued wherfore prayed lorde edmunde irenſyde daye hym ete kyng hym curteyſly graūted hym came prayer meet kyng ryally ſerued dyuerſe mete drynkes whan nyght came ſholde go bedde kyng toke owne meyny went chambre ſhold take nyghtes reſt loked aboute hym ſawe fayre ymage well made ſemblaūt archer bowe bent hande ye bowe fyne arowe kynge edmund went nere beholde better whan anone ye arowe ſmote hym body ſlewe kynge ye engyn made ſlee owne lorde traytourſly whan kynge edmund thus deed ſlayne regned x yere people made moche ſorowe body bare glaſtenbury buryed hym fals traytour edrith anone went ye quene kynge edmundes wyfe wyſt lordes deth toke two ſones fayre yonge lorde goten one called edwarde edwyne ladde wt hym london toke kyng knoght yt ſholde wyl told hȳ ſubtylly ſlayne king edmund bycauſe ye knoght ſholde haue londe englonde ¶ thou fals traytoure haſt yu ſlayne true broder ſo true bycauſe man mooſt loued worlde heed ſhall thy trauayle well rewarde thou haſt deſerued anone let hym taken boūde hym handes foot maner traytour let caſt hym ryuer tamyſe maner fals traytour ended lyfe kyng toke ye two chyldren put vnto abbot weſt mynſter warde kepe tyll wyſt beſt ¶ kynge knoght ſent bothe kyng edmondes ſones denmarke ſlayne ſaued befel ſoone afterward kynge knoght londe handes ſpouſed ye quene emme conſent al baron ſhe fayre woman whiche eldredes wyfe duke ſyſter normandy lyued togyder moche loue reaſon wolde kyng aſked vpon daye coūſeyle quene beſt wt edmond irenſydes ſones syr ſayd ſhe ryght heyres londe yf lyue wyll moche ſorowe wt warre therfore let ſende ſtraūge londe aferre ſome man may deſtroye king anone let call dane called walgar cōmaūded hym ſholde lede thoſe two chyldren denmarke ſo ordeyne ſholde neuer syr ſayd walgar commaūdement gladly ſhall done anone toke two chyldren ledde denmarke moche ſawe chyldren wonder fayre • ke grete pite ruth wold ſlee ledde ye kynge hungary nouryſſhe walgar well beknowen kynge well beloued anone kynge aſked fro whens child walgar tolde hym ſayd yt ye ryght heyres englonde therfore men wolde deſtroye therfore ſyr vnto comen ſeke mercy helpe ſoth yf may lyue men ſhall become ſhall holde theyr londe kynge hungary receyued thē moche honour let worthely kepte thus befell afterwarde edwyne ye yonger broder dyed edwarde elder broder lyued fayre man ſtronge large body gentyll curteys condicyons ſo yt men loued hym edwarde ye cronycles called amonge englyſſhmen edwarde outlawe whan made knyght kynges doughter hungary loued moche goodnes fayrnes ſo ſhe called hym derlynge kynge fader perceyued well loue bytwene two none heyr onely doughter kynge vouchedſafe doughter man ſo well dyd hym ſhe loued ſo well agayn gaue vnto hym good wyll edwarde ſpouſed moche honour kyng hungary ſent baron made ſolemp • e feeſt ryche weddynge made men vnderſtande yt edwarde ſholde kyng deceſſe londe hungary whiche tydynges ryght glad edwarde begate vpon lady ſone whiche called edgar helyng afterwarde doughter called margarete afterwarde quene scotlonde kyng ſcotlond called mancolin ſhe doughter called maud quene afterwarde englonde kyng henry y• fyrſt ſone conquerour wedded begate doughter called maud afterward empreſſe almayne maud came kyng englonde vnto daye called henry empreſſe ſone yet edwarde doughter wyfe yt called chriſtian ſhe nonne ¶ kynge knoght yt proude man conquered way became afterwarde meke mylde haue ye herde edmunde irenſydes ſones yt king knoght wende ben ſlayne cō maūded walgar kyng knoght handes y• realme englond denmark went vnto norway cōquere londe kynge londe yt called elaf came people wende haue well kepte defended londe ſo faught wt hym tyll y• laſt ſlayne yt batayle thā knoght toke y• londe hādes whā cōquered norway takē feaute homage came agayne englonde helde hȳſelfe ſo grete lorde yt hym thought worlde pere became ſo proude hauteyne grete wonder ¶ ſo befell vpon daye herd maſſe weſt mynſter wolde haue gone palays wawes tamyſe ſo ſwyftely came agaynſt hym y• almooſt touched foot ſayd y• kyng proude herte cōmaunde water turne agayn elles ſhall make wawes cōmaūdemēt wold ſpare flowed heyght kyng ſo proude herte wold flee y• water abode ſtyll y• water bette wt yerde y• hande cōmaūded ye water yt ſholde go ferder cō maūdement y• water wold ceſe encreaſed ſo kyng wete ſtode depe water whan ſawe water wold cōmaūdement wtdrewe hym ſtode vpon ſtone holdyng vp handes hye ſayd herynge y• people god yt maketh y• ſee thus aryſe hye kyng kynges mygh te mooſt caytyf deedly man may neuer dye thynge doth cōmaūdement hym obeyeth yt god praye yt warraūt knowlege caytyf feble power therfore wyll go vnto rome without ony longe lettyng wycked ne punyſſhe amende god clay londe holde none anone made redy heyre hȳſelfe went rome without ony lettynge y• waye dyd many almes dedes rome alſo whā ben done penaūce ſynnes came agayn englonde became good man holy leuyng maner pryde lyued holy lyfe made two abbey ſaynt benet one englonde another norway cauſe loued ſaynt benet ſpecyally ony ſaȳt loued moche alſo ſaynt edmund kyng often gaue grete gyftes hous made ryche whan regned xx yere dyed lyeth wyncheſtre ¶ anno dn̄i xviij benedictꝰ ix pope iohannes grete lethour therfore dampned appered certayne man vnder meruaylous fygure horryble heed tayle lyke aſſe part body lyke beer ſayd mā appered aferde man ye beeſtly lyuynge whā pope appere lyke beeſt ¶ mānes tyme grete diuiſyon ſclaūdre y• chirche put two tymes ptholomeus noteth yt pryde byſſhops euer euyl ende euer y• occaſyon moche vnreſt batayle ¶ cōradus fyrſt emperour hēry xx yere mā made many lawes cōmaū ded pea kept mooſt ſtraytly ony man y• erle ludolf accuſed fledde frō londe deſyred lyue lyke chorle lyke gentylman yet meruaylouſly ſone made emperour y• cōmaundement god agaynſt wyl conradus laſt accorded toke conradus doughter wyfe ¶ kynge harold leuer go fote ryde horſbacke knoght whome haue ſpokē two ſones wyfe emme yt one called hardiknoght yt harold ſo lyght fote yt men called hym comynly harold hare fote harold thynge manerd knoght fader ſet cheualry curteyſy ne worſhip onely owne wyll became ſo wicked yt exiled moder emme ſhe went flaū dres dwelled wt y• erle wherfore broder hated echeother deedly whan regned ij yere hedyed lyeth weſt mynſter ¶ kynge hardiknoght haroldes broder harold hare fote regned broder hardyknoght noble knight worthy moche loued cheualry maner goodnes whan hardiknoght regned lytell whyle let vncouer broder harold ſmote heed made caſt gonge body ta myſe came fyſſhers toke y• bedy theyr nettes nyght bare hym ſaynt clemētes chirche buryed hym thus auenged hym hardiknoght broder thus kyng har diknoght ſo large gyuer meet drynke table ſet euery daye thre tymes full ryall mete drynkes meyny came courte kyng hardiknoght ſent emme moder made come agayn broder harold hare fote dryuen y• lond coūſeyle y• erle godwyn greteſt lorde englonde nexte kynge mooſt rule bycauſe ſpouſed doughter kyng knoght begoten fyrſt wyfe whan quene dryuen englond came erle flaundres called baldewyne coſyn foūde thȳge neded vnto tyme ſhe went agayne englonde kynge hardiknoght ſent ſone made come agayne moche honour kyng hardiknoght whan regned v yere dyed lyeth weſt mynſter ¶ vylany dane dyd englyſſhmen wherfore fro tyme dane made kynge londe deth kyng hardiknoght moche ne chylde body begoten •• le baron aſſeinbled made coūſeyl neuer man yt dane though neuer ſo grete man amonge ſhold neuer kyng englonde y• deſpyte yt done englyſſhmen euer yf englyſhmen da ne happened mete vpō brydge englyſhmen ſhold ſo hardy mene fote ſtande ſtyll tyll dane paſſed forth ouer yf englyſhmen bowed theyr heedes reuerence vnto dane ſholde haue ben beten defouled ſuche deſpytes vylany dyd dane englyſſhmē wherfore driuen y• londe hardiknoghtes deth lorde y• myght mayntayne maner auoyded dane englonde neuer came agayn erles baron theyr comyn aſſent counſeyle ſente vnto normādy ſeke thoſe two bretherne alured edwarde dwellynge wt duke rycharde y• theyr vncle entent crowne alured elder broder make hym kyng englonde thynge make ende erles baron made theyr othe erle godwyn weſtſex falſly traytourſly thought ſlee theſe two bretherne anone ſhold come englond entent make harold ſone kynge whiche ſone begoten wyfe kyng hardiknogh te doughter y• dane ſo godwyn went pryuely ſouthhamton mete two bretherne theyr landynge thus befell yt meſſengers yt went normandy foūde onely alured y• eldeſt broder edwarde broder gone hungary ſpeke coſyn edwarde outlawe y• edmund irenſydes ſone meſſengers ſaid aluted y• erles ba ron englond ſent hȳ y• ſhold boldly come englōde receyue realme king hardiknoght deed dane dryuen londe ¶ godwyn fals traytour toke alured vpon gildeſdown whan came normandye kynge englonde cauſed hym martyred yle ely whan alured herd theſe tydȳges thāked god toke ſhyppyng y• haſte myght paſſed ſee arryued ſouth hamton godwyn y• fals traytour whan traytour ſawe y• comen welcomed hym receyued hym moche ioye ſayd yt wold lede hym london baron englonde hym abode make hym theyr kynge ſo went theyr waye towarde london whan came gyldeſdowne tho ſayd y• traytour godwyn vnto alured take hepe aboute bothe lefte ſyde ryght ſyde ye ſhal kyng ſuche hondred mod forſothe ſayd alured behyght yf kyng ſhall ordeyne make ſuche lawes wherof god man ſhall well apayed tray tour cōmaūded men wt hym whan comen vpon gyldeſdown ſhold ſlee aluredes company came hym normādy take alured lede hym y• yle ely put bothe eyen heed afterward brynge hym deth ſo dyd ſlewe y• company nombre xij gentylmen y• comen alured frō normandy toke alured yle ely put eyen rent wombe toke y• chefe bowel put ſtake groūde ende bowel faſtened therto nedyls yren pricked y• good thylde ſo made hym go aboute ſtake tyll yt bowel drawen body ſo dyed alured treaſon erle godwyne whan lordes englond herde wyſt alured ſholde haue ben theyr king put deth fals traytour godwyne wonder wroth ſwore bytwene god holy name ſholde dye worſe deth thā dyd edryth ſtration y• betrayed lorde edmund iren ſyde wold haue put hym deth traytour fledde then denmarke helde hym iiij yere loſt londe englonde silueſter thyrde pope benedictus silueſter choſen benedict expulſed afterwarde silueſter expulſed benedict put vp agayn put gregory made pope ſymple lettred man therfore choſe pope cōſecrate wt hym whan many men dyſpleaſed guydyng two pope thyrde brought whiche ſholde occupy y• place bothe y• two ſo ſtroue amonge ſelfe henry emperour came rome depoſed made clement ſecond pope whome made anone crowne hym ſayd romayns ſholde neuer wtout aſſent choſe pope ſo v beynge pope ſyxth put many men ſaye grego ry holy man ¶ damaſus ſecond clement xxiij dayes man vſurper y• popery che dyed ſodeynly anone romayns aſked haue pope almayns ſholde haue none ſo harde herted myght enclyne entent y• emperout whiche ſayd ſholde pope choſen yf wolde counſeyle eleccyon put holy man leo conſcyence refuſed anone choſen y• comyn aſſent leo put chryſt forme laſar owne bedde morowe founde thynge ¶ ſaynt edwarde confeſſour aluredes broder kynge englonde whā done baron englond ſent another tyme normandy y• edward ſholde come englond moche • onout edwarde chyldhode loued 〈◊〉 hey god hym dradde honeſte clennes ladde lyfe hated ſynne deth whan crow ned anoynted wt ryall power forgate good maners condicyons fyrſt vſed forgate good cuſtomes maner honour ne rycheſſe ne maner hygnes euer gaue hym goodnes well loued god holy chirche paſſyng maner thynge poore men alſo loued helde ben owne bretherne ofte gaue grete almes wt full good wyll ¶ fyrſt ſpecyall loue god ſhewed ſaynt edward lyuynge befell daye went frō chirche weſtmynſter herde maſſe ſaynt iohn ye euangelyſt moche loued ſaȳt iohn euangeliſt ſpecyally god lady dyd ony ſaynt ſo came hym pylgrym prayed hym ye loue god lady ſaynt iohn euangelyſt ſome good gyue hym kyng pryuely toke rynge fynger yt man perceyued gaue pilgrym receyued went then king edward made ye good lawes englonde yet ben mooſt vſed holden ſo mercyable ſo full pyte man myght ¶ erle godwyn came agayne englonde agayne londe afterwarde ſaynt edwarde wedded doughter whan erle godwyn dwellynge denmark moche herde goodnes kynge edwarde full mercy pyte thought yt wolde go agayne englond ſeke haue grace good kyng edward ſo mercy full myght haue agayn londe pea arayed hym moche myght put hym towarde ſee came englonde london ye kynge tyme lordes englonde helde parlyamēt godwyn ſent yt frendes ye mooſt greteſt lordes lōde prayed beſeche ye kynges grace hym wolde graunte pea lōde lordes lad hȳ ye kyng ſeke grace anone ye kyng ſawe hym appeled hym treaſon deth alured broder theſe wordes hym ſayd traytour godwyn appele thou haſt betrayed ſlayne broder alured certes ſyr ſayd godwyn ſaue grace pea lordſhyp neuer betrayed hym • e yet lewe hȳ therfore put reward caurte fayre lordes ſayd ye kynge ye lyeges erles baron londe yt ben aſſembled full well ye herde myn appele anſwere alſo godwyn therfore wyll ye awarde ryght erles baron gadred togyder awarde themſelfe ſo ſpake dy uerſly among ſome ſayd neuer alyaūce homage ſerment ſeruyce lordſhyp bytwene godwyn alured whiche thynge myght hym drawe laſt deuyſed demed ſhold put hym ye kynges mercy togyder thā ſna ke erle leuerike couentre good man god worlde told reaſon maner ſayd erle godwyn ye beſt frended man englonde ye kyng well myght gaynſayd without cou • ſe yle godwyn alured neuer put deth wherfore awarde touchynge parte hymſelf ſone euery v xii erles ben frendes go kynge charged moche golde ſyluer may bere bytwene handes prayenge kynge forgyue euyll wyll erle godwyn receyue homage yelde agayn londe accorded vnto awarde came euery golde ſyluer moche myght bere bytwene theyr handes kynge ſayd forme maner theyr accorde theyr awarde kyng wolde gaynſaye moche ordeyned graūted cōfermed ſo erle godwyn accorded kynge agayne londes afterward bare hym ſo well ſo wyſely kynge loued hym wonder moche hym full preuy within lytell tyme loued ſo moche ye kynge ſpouſed godwyns doughter made quene neuertheles though kyng wyfe yet lyued euer chaſtite clennes body wtout ony fleſſhely dede doynge wyfe ye quene alſo halfe ladde holy lyfe two yere dyed afterwarde kynge lyued lyfe without ony wyfe kyng gaue erledome oxford harolde godwyns ſone made hym erle ſo well beloued bothe ye fader ſo preuy kynge yt myght ryght thynge wolde agaynſt ryght wold thynge maner man ſo good true conſcyence therfore lorde ieſu chryſt ſpecyall loue ſhewed hym ¶ kynge edwarde ſawe •• wyne kynge denmarke drowned ſee tyme leuacyon ſacrament ſtode herde maſſe befell vpon whytſondaye kynge edwarde herde maſſe grete chirche weſtmynſter leuacion ieſu chriſtes body men gadred chirche came nigh awter ſe ye ſacrynge kyng lyft vp handes hygh toke vp grete laughter wherfore yt ſtode aboute hym began gretly wonder maſſe aſked kȳges laughter fayre lordes ſaid kynge edward ſawe swyne ye yonger kyng denmarke come ſee wt power haue comen englond warre vpon v ſawe hym folke drowned ſee ſawe leuacyon chryſtes body bytwene preeſtes hādes therof ſo grete wye myght laughter withholde erle leuerich ſtode beſyde hym leuacion openly ſawe forme breed turne ye lykenes yonge childe toke vp ryght hande blyſſed kynge afterwarde ye erle erle anone turned hym toward ye kynge make hym ſe holy ſyght ſayd kynge syr erle ſo well ye ſe thanked god haue honoured god ſauyour vyſybly ieſu chryſt forme man whoſe na blyſſed worldes amen ¶ rynge ſaynt edwarde gyuen poore pylgrym ye loue god ſaynt iohn euangelyſt came agayne kynge edwarde noble man ſaynt edwarde regned xiii yere thus fell vpon tyme dyed ye two men englond gone ye holy londe done theyr pilgrymage goynge agayne theyr owne coūtree came fro went waye mette pilgrym curteyſly ſalewed aſked londe coūtree borne ſayd englonde aſked kyng englonde anſwered ſayd good king edward fayre frendes ſayd pylgrym whan ye come coūtree agayne praye ye wyll go vnto kyng edwarde greet hym oftentymes name oftenty me thanke grete curteyſy yt hath done namely ye ryng yt gaue whan herde maſſe weſtmynſter ſaynt iohns loue ye euāgelyſt toke ye rynge toke pylgryms ſayd praye go bere ryng take vnto kyng edward tell hym ſende hym full ryche gyfte wyll gyue hym vpō xij daye ſhal come euermore dwell blyſſe wtouten ende syr ſayd ye pilgryms man ye coūtree dwellynge fayre frendes ſayd iohn euangelyſt dwellynge almyghty god kynge edward frende loue hym ſpecyall bycauſe hath euermore lyued clennes clene mayd praye meſſage fulfyll haue ſayd whan ſaȳt iohn ye euāgelyſt thus charged ſodeynly voyded bothe theyr ſightes thanked ye pylgryms almyghty god went forth theyr waye whan gone two thre myle begā ware wery ſet reſt ſo fell ſlepe whan well ſlepte one awoke lyft vp heed loked aboute ſayd felowe aryſe vp go waye ſayd felowe certes ſayd ye ſemeth yt ye ſame coūtre layde v • owne reſt ſlepe ieruſalem thre myles toke vp theyr handes blyſſed went forth theyr waye went ſawe ſhepes herdes goyng wt theyr ſhepe ſpake none lāguage engliſſhe good frendes ſayd one ye pylgryms coūtre lord therof anone ſhepeherdes anſwered ſayd coūtree kent englond whiche good kynge edward lorde pilgryms thanked almyghty god ſaynt iohn ye euangelyſt went forth theyr waye came caunterbury then london foūde kynge tolde hym ye begynnynge endynge moche ſaynt iohn charged thȳges ſpēdde ye waye toke ye rynge kyng edward receyued thanked almyghty god ſaynt iohn ye euan gelyſt made hym redy euery daye daye daye departe lyfe whan god wold ſend hym ¶ ſaynt edwarde dyed xij daye befel thus chryſt maſſe euen holy man edward goddes ſeruyce matyns ye hygh feeſt became full ſeke morowe endured wt moche payne ye maſſe maſſe let hym ladde chambre reſt hym hall amonge baron knyghtes myght come comforte ſolace wont worthy feeſt wherfore theyr myrth cōforte amonge hall turned care ſorowe bycauſe drad leſe theyr cyte acre whan taken dwelled ye cite whyle hym came tydynges ye erle iohn oxford broder wolde haue ſeaſed englonde handes normandy alſo wolde crowne hym ſelfe kynge londe whan kyng rychard herde theſe raunſom payed eche chalice englōd molten made money monkes ordre ciſteaux gaue theyr bokes englonde ſolde paye raunſom ¶ kynge rychard came agayn ye holy londe auenged hym enemyes whyles kyng rycharde pryſon kynge fraunce warred vpon hȳ ſtrongly mandy iohn broder warred vpon hym englond ye byſſhops baron englond withſtode hym ye power myght gete toke caſtell wyndſore caſtelles foreſayd iohn ſawe might ne power agaynſt baron englond fyght anone wente hym ouer ſee vnto kynge fraūce whan kynge rycharde came pryſon delyuered came englond anone candelmaſſe grete haſte went vnto notyngham caſtell notingham hym yelded diſcomfyted broder iohn thoſe held hym went vnto cyte wyncheſtre let hym crowned kynge englonde went vnto mandy warre vpon kynge fraūce whan kyng fraūce herde came fyur hondred knyghtes towarde gyſors kynge rycharde mette hym wolde haue gyuen hym batayle kynge fraūce anone fledde hondred knyghtes taken two hondre horſes trapped • en ¶ anone went kyng rychard beſyege caſtell gayllard vpon daye rode caſtell take auyſement caſtell one arbalaſtres ſmore hym quarell enuenymed kyng richard drewe ſhafte quarell quarelles heed abode ſtyll heed began rankle myght helpe hymſelfe ne meue armes whan wyſt dethes wounde vpon hym myght hole maner thynge cōmaūded anone men ſharply aſſayle caſtell ſo ye caſtell takē ye dyed ſo māly men dyd taken ye wtin kyng dyd wt wyl cōmaūded men brȳge hȳ man ye ſo woūded hym whan came hym kynge aſked hym name ſaid name bertrā gurdon wherfore ſayd ye king haſt ye ſlayne ſyth dyd ye neuer harme syr ſayd people bachelers gaſcoyns ſoudyours dwellynge wt iohn veſſye hym receyued wage hym holden noble men fyght brent many townes ſlewe ye walſhmen myght take thoſe wt ſtrength myght made aſſaute vnto caſtell swandon gate caſtell whā dauid herde theſe tydynges ordeyned hȳ flyght whā lewlyn ye prynce knewe broder fledde thā ſore abaſſhed power warre maynteyn ſo lewlyn began flee wende well haue ſcaped mornyng ſyr roger mortimer mette wt hym onely x knightes ſet hym roūde aboute hym went ſmote heed preſented kyng edward maner lewlyn ye prynce wale taken heed ſmytten alſo heyres dyſheryted euermore ryghtfull dome lordes realme ¶ dauid yt lewlyns broder prynce wale put deth dauid ye prynces broder wale pride wende haue bē prynce wale broders deth vpō ſent walſhmen patlyament dinbigh folyſſhly made wale aryſe agaynſt ye kyng began meue warre agaynſt kyng edward dyd ye ſorowe dyſeaſe myght power whan kynge edward herde thynge ordey ned men purſue vpon hym dauid fyer • hym defended tyll yt came ye towne ſaynt morite dauid taken fledde ladde kynge kyng cōmaūded ſhold hanged drawen ſmyte heed quarter hȳ ſende heed london foure quarter foure chefe townes wale ſholde take enſample therof ware afterward kynge edward let crye pea though al wale ſeaſed ye londe handes ye grete lordes lefte alyue came feaute homage kynge edward theyr kynde lorde let kynge edward amende lawes wale yt defectyue ſent al ye lordes wale lettres patentes yt ſholde come parlyamēt whan comen kynge ſayd full curteyſly lordes ye welcome behoueth coūſeyle helpe go gaſcoyn amende ye treſpace done whan entreate pea bytwene ye kynge aragon prȳce morrey ye kynges liege men erles baron conſented graūted therto kynge edwarde made hym redy went gaſcoyn let amende ye treſpaces yt done hȳ gaſcoyn ye debate bytwene ye kyng aragon prynce morrey ceſſed accorded whyle kynge edward quene elenore wyfe gaſcoyn good erle cornewayle made wardeyn englonde tyll kyng edward came agayn thā enquyred tray tour yt coniected falſnes agaynſt hym eche thē receyued theyr dome deſerued meane tyme whyle kyng edward beyonde yt ſee make amendes yt treſpaced agaynſt hȳ fals traytour yt called • iſap meridoc began make warre agaynſt kynge edward cauſe ſyr payne tiptot ye wrongfully greued diſeaſed ye foreſayd biſap meridoc whan kynge edward herde ſente lettres biſap meridoc ſholde make warre ſholde pea loue whan came agayne englonde wolde vndertake ye quarell amende myſdone foreſayd riſap meridoc deſpyſed kynges cō maundement ſpared ſorowe myght ye kynges men englond anone taken ladde yorke drawen hanged felony ¶ redreſſyng king edward made iuſtices clerkes done theyr falſnes droue ye iewes englonde theyr vſury myſbyieue whan kynge edward dwelled thre yere gaſcoyn deſyre came hȳ go englonde agayn whan comen agayn ſo many cōplayntes made hym iuſtices clerkes done ſo many wronges falſnes wonder whiche falſnes ſyr thomas weylonde kynges iuſtyce forſwore englonde ye toure londō falſnes men put vpon hym wherof atteynt proued fals anone whan kynge done wyll iuſtices let enquyre eſpye iewes deceyued begyled people theyr ſynne falſnes vſury let ordeyn preuy parliament amonge lordes ordeyned amōge ye iewes ſhold voyde eng lōde theyr miſbyleue alſo theyr falſe vſury dyd vnto chryſten men ſpede make ende thynge comynalte englonde gaue vnto kynge xv peny al theyr goodes mouable ſo iewes dryuen englonde went ye iewes fraūce dwelled leue kyng philyp kynge fraūce ¶ kynge edwarde ſeaſed ye londe scotlonde cōſent graūte ye lordes scotlonde longe ye alexander kyng scotlonde deed dauid erle huntingdon kynges broder scotlond aſked claymed ye kingdom scotlonde broder deed bycauſe rightfull heyre many grete lordes ſayd naye wherfore grete debate aroſe bytwene theyr fren de moche wolde con ſent crownacyon meane tyme foreſayd dauid dyed ſo befell yt ſayd dauid thre dough ters worthely maryed fyrſt doughter maryed bayloll ſeconde brus thyrde haſtynges foreſayd bayloll brus chalenged ye londe scotlonde grete debate ſtryfe aroſe bytwene thre bycauſe eche wolde haue ben kyng whan ye lordes scotlonde ſawe ye debate bytwene came kyng edward englonde ſeaſed hym ye londe scotlonde chefe lord whan kyng ſeaſed foreſayd lordes scotlonde ye foreſayd bayloll brus haſtynges came kynges courte aſked ye kynge whiche ſholde kyng scotlonde kyng edward full gentyll true let enquyre cronycles scotlonde greteſt lordes scotlonde whiche ye eldeſt blode foūde yt bayloll eldeſt kyng scotlonde ſhold holde ye kyng englonde hym feaute homage done bayloll went scotlonde crowned kynge scotlond ye ſame tyme vpon ſee grete warre bytwene ye englyſſh men norman vpon tyme normās arryued douer martyred holy man yt called thomas douer afterward norman ſlayne yt eſcaped one ¶ ſoone kynge edward ſholde leſe duchy gaſcoyn kyng philip fraū ce fals caſtyng ye dou • e peres lond wherfore ſyr edmond kyng edwardes broder gaue vp homage vnto ye kyng fraūce ¶ yt tyme ye clerkes englonde graūted kynge edward halfe dele holy chirche goodes helpynge recouer londe agayn gaſcoyn kynge ſent thyder noble company bachelers hymſelfe wolde haue gone porteſinouth letted one maddok wale yt ſeaſed caſtell swandon handes cauſe ye kyng turned wale chryſtmaſſe bycauſe noble lordes englond yt ſent gaſcoyn cōfort theyr lorde kyng taken ſyr charles fraūce ſay ſyr iohn brytayne ſyr robert typtot ſyr raufe tanny ſyr hugh bardulf ſyr adam cretynge yet ye aſcencyon maddok taken wale another whiche called morgan ſent toure london byheded ¶ ſyr iohn bailoll kyng scotlonde withſayd homage whā ſyr iohn bailoll kyng scotlonde vnderſtode yt kyng edwarde warred gaſcoyne whome ye realme scotlonde delyuered falſly agaynſt othe wt ſayd homage procuryng folke ſent vnto courte rome fals ſuggeſtion aſſoyled othe yt ſwore vnto kynge englonde ſo lettre embulled ¶ choſe scotlonde douſpers take edward ryght ¶ yt tyme came two cardynals rome fro ye pope celeſtyne treate accorde bytwene kyng fraūce kyng englonde thoſe cardynals ſpake accorde thomas turbeluyl taken lyon made feaute homage warden parys hym put two ſones hoſtage thought go englonde eſpye coūtre tell whan came englonde yt broken kynges priſon fraūce nyght ſayd wolde yt englyſſhmen walſhmen ſholde aboute ye kyng fraūce thynge bryng ende ſwore vpon couenaūt dedes made bytwene ſholde haue yere poūdes worth londe brȳge thynge ende fals traytour toke leue went then came englōde vnto ye kyng ſayd yt broken pryſon put hȳ ſuche peryl loue wherfore ye kynge coude hȳ moche thanke full glad comynge fals traytour fro yt daye eſpyed doynge ye kynge alſo coū ſeyle kynge loued hym well wt hym full preuy clerke englonde yt kynges hous fraūce herde treaſon falſnes wrote clerke dwellyng wt kyng edward englonde thomas turbeluyll done fals conife • tynge coūſeyle englonde wryten haue ſent vnto ye king fraūce foreſayd lettre ye clerke ſent fro fraūce foūde vpon hym wher fore ladde london hāged drawen robert roos batwyk dedde fro ye englyſſhmen went scottes kyng edward went toward barwyk beſyeged towne yt within māly defended ſet fyre brent two kyng edwardes ſhyppes ſayd deſpyte repre • e hym hym viij dayes reſpyte myght ſende tell ſyr iohn bayloll kyng scotlonde men fared within ye caſtell ſent hym worde yf wolde remeue ſyege englyſſhmen wolde yelde caſtell englyſſhmen meſſenger came vnto ſyr iohn bailoll ye kynge scotlonde hooſt meſſenger tolde hym caſe ſyr iohn bayloll toke hooſt came morowe erly towarde caſtell ſyr rychard sywarde ſawe hym come mayſter coūſeyle keper ye caſtell spenſer cō maūded anone bynde hym haſte went agaynſt theyr enemyes ſlewe scottes nombre xxij scottes tyme man honour ſaue ſyr patryk graham manly fought longe laſt ſlayne ſayd englyſſhmen reprefe scottes theſe ſcaterand scottes holde ſottes wrench vnware erly mornynge euyll tymyng went ye fro dunbare ¶ whan thoſe yt caſtell ſawe dyſcōfyture yelded vp caſtell ye englyſſhe men boūde theyr bodyes londes caſtels kynge edward ſo taken ye caſtell thre erles vij ba ron xxviij knyghtes xj clerkes vij pycardes preſented kyng edward ſent ye toure london kepte ¶ kynge edward grete grace delyuered agayne scottes pryſon chefetaynes londe drewe frenſſhmen coūſeyle wyllyam waleys whan kynge edward made ende warre taken chefetaynes scotlond came ſyr iohn bayloll wt yelded vnto kyng edward put grace ladde london whā kyng edward comen thyder brought hȳ ye kynge aſked wolde make amendes treſpace loſſe yt done put mercy lordes ſayd kyng wyll londes ne goodes wyll yt ye make othe vpō goddes body true neuer tyme agaynſt bere armes conſented kynges wyll ſwore vpon goddes body yt ſay ſyr iohn comyn ye erle strathorne ye erle ca • yk alſo iiij biſſhops vndertoke al clergy ſo ye kynge delyuered gaue ſafeconduytes go theyr owne coūtree lōge afterwarde aroſe agaynſt kyng edward bycauſe wyſt well kynge edwardes folke taken gaſcoyn ſayd ſyr iohan bayloll kynge scotlonde wyſt well londe ſholde haue ſorowe ynough ſhame theyr falſnes haſte went hym ouer ye ſee owne londes helde hym neuer came agayne wherfore ye scottes choſe vnto theyr kyng willyam waleys rybaud harlot comen vp nought englyſſhmen dyd moche harme ¶ kyng edward thought myght beſt delyuer people taken gaſcoyne haſte went hym ouer ſee flaundres warre vpon kyng fraunce erle flaūdres receyued hym moche honour graūted hym londes owne wyl whan kyng fraūce herde tell yt kyng englond arryued flaūdres came wt huge power deſtroye hym prayed hȳ trewſe two yere ſo ye englyſſhe marchaūtes alſo frenſſhe myght ſafely go come bothe ſydes kynge edwarde graūted ſo yt men priſon yt gaſcoyn ye kyng fraūce graūted anone ſo delyuered ¶ ſame tyme scottes ſent byſſhop ſaynt andrewes fraūce ye kyng ſyr charles broder yt ſyr charles ſhold come wt power scotlond wolde come wt theyr power ſo ſholde go englonde ye lond • deſtroye scotlond vnto • en • ſcottes truſted moche vpon ye frenſſh men yt thȳge maner graūte yet neuertheleſſe ye scottes began robbe ſlee northumberlonde dyd moche harme ¶ willyam waleys let ſlee ſyr hugh creſſingham batayle fonkirke whan tydynges came kyng edward wyllyam waleys ordeyned ſuche ſtronge power alſo scotlonde hym attendaunt redy ſlee englyſſhmen deſtroye londe ſore anoyed ſent anone lettre ye erle garren ſyr henry percy ſyr willyam latomer ſyr hugh creſſyngham treſourer ſholde take power go northumberlonde ſo forth scotlond kepe coūtrees whan willyam waleys herde theyr comynge began flee ye englyſſhmen folowed hym droue hym tyll came • ry uelyn helde hym ye caſtell walſhmen euery daye eſcryed thretened dyd deſpyte myght ſo yt englyſſhmen vpon tyme mornyng went frō caſtel mountenaūce x myle paſſed ouer brydge william waleys came ſtronge power droue backe englyſſhmen power agaynſt hym fledde yt myght take brydge eſcaped ſyr hugh kynges treſourer ſlayn many alſo wherfore made moche ſorowe ¶ kyng edward ſpedde mater flaū dres comen agayn englōde haſtely toke waye scotlonde came thyder ye aſcencyon tyde foūde ſet fyre brent ye poore people scotlonde came hym wonder thycke prayed hym goddes loue haue mercy wherfore kyng cōmaūded yt man ſhold harme yt yoldē hym ne mā ordre hous religion ne maner chirche let eſpye yt myght fynde ony enemyes came ſpye ye kynge tolde hȳ scottes aſſembled abyde batayle ſo ſaynt mary magdaleyns day ye kynge came fonkirk gaue batayle ye scottes ye batayle ſlayne xxxiij ſcottes englyſhmen xxviij mo yt whiche worthy knight ſlayne hoſpytaler yt called frere brian iay whan william waleys fled ye batayle ſame brian hym purſued fyerſly hors ran ſtart myre mary vp ye bely willyā waleys turned agayne ſlewe ſyr bryan yt grete harme whyle kynge edwarde went scotlonde enquyre yf myght fynde ony enemyes ye londe dwelled longe hym lyked none enemy durſt abyde ſoone yt kyng edward went southamton wolde abyde scotlond wynter ſeaſon eſement people whan came london let amende many • dedes done agaynſt pea lawes whyle flaūdres ¶ laſt maryage kyng edward went thyrde tyme scotlonde afterward ordeyned court rome kyng edward ſhold wedde dame mar garete kyng philip ſyſter fraūce archebyſſhop robert wynchelſe ſpouſed thē togider whiche mariage made pea bytwene kynge edward englonde kynge philyp fraūce ¶ kynge edwarde went thyrde tyme scotlond wtin ye fyrſt yere famyſſhed londe ſo yt lefte one al came mercy ſaue ye caſtell eſtreuelyn well vitayled ſtored vij yere ¶ caſtell eſtreuelyn beſyeged wonne bynge edward came caſtell eſtreuelyn wt huge power beſyeged caſtell lytel auayled myght scottes harme caſtell ſo ſtronge well kepte whan kyng edward ſawe bethought hym queyntyſe cauſed anone make two payr hye galowes toure ye caſtell made othe many within caſtell erle baron taken ſtrengthe yf wolde rather yelde hym ſholde hanged vpon ye ſame payr galowes whan within caſtell herde came yelded kinges grace mercy kyng forgaue yll wyll ye grete lordes ſcotlonde ſworne kynge edward yt ſholde come london euery parlyament ſholde ſtande ordynaunce troylebaſton fyrſt ordeyned byng edward went then london wende haue reſt pea warre yt whiche warre occupyed xx yere ſay wale gaſtoyn scotlonde thought myght recouer treſour yt ſpended warre let enquyre ye realme tyme yt ben realme men called troylebaſton ordeyned therto iuſtices maner recouered treſour wtout nombre purpoſe haue gone holy londe haue warred vpon goddes enemyes bycauſe croſſed longe tyme neuertheles lawe yt ordeyned dyd moche good englonde myſbode thoſe yt treſpaced well chaſtyſed afterwarde moche meker better poore comyns reſt pea ye ſame tyme king edward priſoned owne ſone edwarde bycauſe ye byſſhop cheſtre ye kynges treſourer complayned hȳ ſayeng yt coū ſeyle one pyers ganaſton ſquyer gaſcoyn broken parkes pyers coūſeyled ladde ſame edward cauſe kynge edward exiled pyers englōde ¶ deth willyam waleys fals traytour whan kynge edward ouercomen enemyes wale gaſcoyn scotlonde deſtroyed traytours ſaue onely ye rybaud willyā waleys ye neuer wolde yelde hym ye kyng ye laſt taken towne ſaynt dominyk xxxiij yere king edwardes regne preſented kyng edward kyng wolde ſe hym ſent hym london receyue iudgement vpō ſaynt barthylmewes euen hanged drawen heed ſmytten bowelles taken body brent body quartred ſent foure beſt townes scotlonde heed put vpon ſpere ſet vpō london brydge enſample yt scottes ſholde haue mynde amyſſe agaynſt theyr lyege lorde agayne ¶ scottes came kyng edward amende theyr treſpace done agaynſt hym michelmas next comyng kyng edward helde parlyament weſtmynſter thyder came ye scottes ſaye byſſhop ſaynt andrewes robert brus erle carik symond friſell iohn ye erle athell accorded ye kyng bounde othe ſwore yf ony afterward myſbare agaynſt kynge ſholde diſheryted euermore whā theyr pea thus made toke theyr leue went home vnto theyr coūtree ¶ robert brus chalenged scotlonde robert brus erle • aryk ſent lettres vnto erles baron scotlonde ſhold come hym sconne morowe coucepcyon lady grete nedes londe lordes came ye daye aſſygned ſame daye ſyr robert brus ſayd fayre lordes full well ye knowe yt perſone dwelleth ryght realme scotlonde ye well wote ryghtfull heyre ſyth yt ſyr iohn baylon kynge hath forſaken v left londe though ſo kyng edward englond wrongfull power hath made aſſent hym agaynſt wyll yf yt ye wyll graunt yt may kynge scotlonde ſhall kepe agaynſt king edward englonde agaynſt maner men yt worde abbot sconne aroſe vp ſayd yt reaſon helpe hym defende ye londe ſayd wolde gyue hym poūde maynteyn ye londe ye graūted hym londe theyr power hym helpe defyed kynge edwarde englonde ſayd yt robert brus ſholde kyng scotlonde ¶ ſyr iohn comyn gaynſayd crownynge ſyr robert brus ¶ ordynges ſayd ſyr iohn comyn thynke ye trouth othe ye made kyng edward englōd touchyng ſelfe wyll breke myn othe man ſo went wherfore robert ye brus tho cōſented hym yll content wt ſyr iohn comyn thā ordeyned another coūſeyle domfris came ye foreſayd ſyr john comyn dwelled two myle domfris wont ſoiourne abyde ¶ ſyr john comyn traytourſly ſlayne whā robert brus wyſt grete lordes scot lōde come scōne ſaue ſyr iohn comyn abode nygh scōne ſent ſpecially ſayd ſyr iohn comyn come ſpeke hym vpon came ſpake wt gray freres domfris thurſday candelmaſſe daye ſyr iohn graūted go wt hym whan herde maſſe toke ſoppe dranke afterward beſtrode pa • frey rode domfris whan robert brus ſawe hym come wynow chambre made toye ynough came agaynſt hym colled hym necke made hym good ſemblaūt whan erles baron scotlond preſent robert ye brus ſayn ſyrs ye wote well cauſe comynge wher fore yf ye wyll graūte may kyng scotlonde ryght heyre londe ye lordes yt ſayd wt one voyce yt ſholde crowned kyng scotlond yt wolde helpe hȳ maynteyn agaynſt men lyuyng dye hym yfnede gentyl ſo ordeyned englond kyng coūſeyle quene iſabell ſholde go fraūce treate pea bytwene lorde broder olyuer yngham ſholde go gaſcoyn haue hym vij men armes ſeneſſhall wardeyn gaſcoyn ſo ordeyned quene ſyr olyuer yngham went ouer gaſcoyn dyd moche harme kyng fraūce gate agayne kynge edwarde loſt moche therto ¶ kynge edwarde ſent ſyr edward ſone eldeſt fraūce quene iſabell quarter yere dwelled fraunce whan ſyr edward eldeſt ſone aſ •• leue go fraūce ſpeke wt moder iſabell y• quene fader y• kyng graūted hym wt good wyll ſayd hȳ go fayre ſone goddes bleſſyng myne thynke come agayn haſtely herytege maner aunceſtres dyd wherfore called duke guyen ¶ kyng exiled quene iſabell edwarde eldeſt ſone whan kyng edward englonde herde tell y• kynge fraūce gyuen y• duchy guyen ſyr edward ſone wtout cōſent wyll hȳ ſone receyued y• duchy 〈◊〉 became wōders wroth ſent ſone lettre wyfe alſo y• ſh • ld come agayn englonde haſte quene iſabel ſyr edward ſone wonder ſore adrad y• kynges menace ſhold holden enemyes bothe ye realme alſo crowne englond yt wolde come englond bothe exiled moder ſone whan ye quene herd theſe tydynges ſhe ſore adrad deſtroyed fals coniectynge spenſers went wt y• baron englonde whan kynges patent thynge ſhewed lordes ordeyned parliament ſhold weſtmynſter vtas ſaynt hylary grete lordes englonde let ordeyne agaynſt tyme parlyament ſholde whiche daye y• kyng depo ſed ſayd wolde crowne edward ſone y• elder yt duke guyenne ſent tydynges vnto kyng warde vnder ſyr iohn erle garen ſyr iohn bothun yt byſſhop ely ſyr henry percy baron ſyr willyam truſſell knyght y• y• erle thomas lancaſtre yeld vp theyr homage vnto hym englonde ſyr wyllyam truſſell ſayd theſe wordes syr edward bycauſe ye haue betrayed people englond haue vndone many grete lordes englond without ony cauſe ye ſhall depoſed ye withſtande thanked god alſo bycauſe ye wold come y• parliament ye ordeyned weſtmynſter owne lettre patent conteyned treate wt lyege men kyng ſholde therfore y• comyns aſſent lordes englonde tell vnto theſe wordes ye ſhall vnderſtande ſyr baron englond one aſſent wyll ye king englond vtterly haue put ryalte euermore byſſhop ely ſayd kynge syr edwarde yelde vp feaute homage y• archebiſſhops byſſhops englond y• clergy ſayd ſyr iohn erle garen syr edward yelde vp vnto feau te homage y• erles englōde ſyr henry percy gaue vp alſo homage y• baron englonde ſayd ſyr william truſſell yelde vp vnto ſyr myn homage knyghtes englonde y• holde ſergeaūtry ony maner thynge ſo y• day af terward ye ſhall claymed kynge kynge holden tyme afterwarde ye ſhall holden ſinguler man y• people ſo went then london y• lordes englonde abode ſyr edward abode priſon good kepyng daye y• cōuerſyon ſaynt paule xx yere regne ¶ prophery merlyn declared kynge edwarde ſone kynge edward fyrſt kyng edward prophecyed merlin ſayd y• ſholde come gote carre yt ſhold haue horne ſyluer berde whyte ſnowe droppe ſhold come noſethrylles yt ſholde betoken moche harme honger dethe people grece loſſe londe y• begynnynge regne ſholde haūted moche lechery ſayd ſothe ala tyme kyng edward yt kyng edwardes ſone borne carnaruan wale ſothe horne ſyluer berd whyte ſnowe whan made prȳce wale moche gaue hym ryot foly ſothe ſayd merlyn ꝓphecy ſhold come noſe droppe tyme grete honger among y• poore people ſtronge dethe amonge y• ty dyed ſtrange londe ſorowe warre scotlond afterward loſt scotlonde gaſcoyn moche le chery dayes haūced ¶ alſo merlyn ſayd yt gote ſholde ſeke floure lyfe deth ſayd ſo ſpouſed iſabell y• kynges ſyſter fraūce tyme merlyn ſayd ſhold made brydges folk vpon dyches ſee y• well ſeen bannockeſbourne scotlonde whā diſcōtyted y• scotces merlyn tolde alſo ſtones ſholde fall caſtels many townes ſhold made playne ſayd ſothe whan kynge edward diſcomfyted scotlonde came ſouthwarde scottes beſyeged caſtels dyd moche harme brent townes vnto harde erth ¶ afterward merlyn tolde egle ſholde come cornewayle ſholde haue fethers golde pryde ſholde haue pere ſhold deſpyſe lordes blode ſhold dye bere gauerſyche prophecy full well knowen foūde ſoche egle vnderſtande ſyr pyers ganaſton erle cornewayle whiche wonder proude man deſpiſed baron englonde afterward heded gauerſyche ye erle lancaſtre erle warwyk ¶ merlyn tolde tyme ſholde ſeme bere ſholde brenne batayle ſhold vpon arme ſee felde arayed lyke ſhelde ſholde dye many whyte hedes ſayd ſothe brennynge ye bere betokened grete drede cuttynge ſwerdes batayle myton came ye scottes maner ſhelde wynge ſlewe men religyon preeſtes ſeculers wher fore scottes called batayle deſpyte englyſſhmen whyte batayle ¶ merlin ſayd foreſayd bere ſholde gote moche harme yt ſholde vpon ye ſouth weſt alſo vpon blode ſayd alſo yt gote ſhold leſe moche dele londe tyll tyme ſhame ſholde hym ouercome ſhold clothe hym lyon ſkynne ſholde wynne agayne loſt people ſholde come north weſt yt ſholde make hym fered hym auenge vpon enemyes counſeyle two owles fyrſt ſhold peryl vndone thoſe two owles ſholde go ouer ſee ſtraūge londe dwell certayn tyme ſhold returne agayn englond ſhold moche harme many one ſholde coūſeyle ye gote meue warre agaynſt foreſaid bere gote owles ſholde come arme ye ſee burton vpon trent ſholde go ouer drede bere ſholde flee ſwan cōpany bury towarde ye north vnkynde outpulter ye ſwan thā ſhold ſlayne wt ſorow bere ſhold ſlayne full nye owne neſt yt ſhold ſtande vpon poūtfret vpon whome ſonne ſholde ſhede bemes many folke ſhold ſeke hym vertue ſayd ſothe ye good erle thomas lācaſtre borne north weſt coſyn ye kynge vncles ſone lawe made ye kynge leſe moche lōde yt purchaſed wyl fully tyll ye laſt kynge toke therof ſhame hymſelfe fylled wt cruelte gate agayne yt loſt moche helpe folk comyng ye northweſt drad auenged hȳ baron coū ſeyle ye two spēſers yt afore lawed theyr wickednes came agayne fraūce ſo moche theſe spenſers coūſeyled ye kynge yt ſhold warre vpon thomas lancaſtre ſo yt kyng spenſers erle arundell theyr power mette thomas lancaſtre burton vpon trent hym diſcomfyted ſyr vmfrey erle herford company fledde foreſayd thomas vmfrey theyr company burbrygge metynge ſyr andrewe herkela called ye vnkynde outpulter alſo ſyr symond warde erle yorke came met wt thomas lātaſtre wt huge company diſcōſyted y• diſcō ſiture y• crle herford ſlayne vpon brydge cowardly ſpere foūdement erle thomas taken ladde poūtfret heded beſyde owne caſtell afterward many hym ſought myracles y• god dyd hym y• tyme merlyn ſayd ſorowe harme ſholde dye people londe wherfore many londes ſholde vpon hym bolder ſayd ſothe bycauſe baron put deth ſaȳt thomas quarell lancaſtre people many londes became bolder meue warre vpon theyr kyng theyr blode turned many nacyons afterward merlyn tolde ſayd yt foreſayd owles ſholde moche harme vnto floure lyfe deth ſholde brynge moche dyſeaſe ſo ſhe ſholde go ouer ſee fraūce make pea y• floure delyce ſholde abyde tyll tyme ſede ſhold come ſeke ſhold abyde bothe tyll y• tyme ſholde clothe grace thoſe two owles ſhe ſholde ſeke put pyteous deth prophecy well knowen full ſothe ſyr hugh spenſer fader ſyr hugh ſone moche ſorowe perſecucyon vnto quene iſabell theyr ꝓcuremēt lord y• kyng ordeyned ſore adradde come wende haue areſted tyll made amendes treſpace ſyr hugh spenſer fader ſone done y• harme y• done quene iſabell ſyſter wherfore ordynaūce cōſent y• spenſers y• quene iſabell went prelate erles baron ye realme scotlonde wt theyr ſeales ſet theron chartres remembraunces yt kynge edwarde baron theyr right ye foreſayd realme scotlond forgyuen agaynſt holy chirche alſo ye blacke
