laſt scottes bounde vnto kyng xxx poūde ſyluer payed within thre yere euery yere x poūde euen porcyons forthermore aboue ſpake bytwene partyes aboue ſayd dauyd dritonautier kynge robert brus ſone ye fals tyraunt fals forſworne agaynſt othe yt aroſe agaynſt lyege lorde noble good kyng edward falſly made kyng scotlōde ye age v yere ſo curſed counſeyle dauid ſpouſed barwyk dame ione toure kynge edwardes ſyſter ye geſt telleth vpon mary magdaleyns daye ye yere grace ccc xxviij grete harme empayrynge kynges blode wherof gentyll lady came ala ye tyme wonder moche fayre damoyſell deſparaged ſyth scotlonde holden realme englonde feaute ſeruyce aboue ſayd ye cronycles englonde scotlonde bereth wytnes plenarly ¶ curſed tyme parliament holden northamton fals coūſeyle kyng falſly dyſheryted yet within age yet whan kyng edward put royalte englonde yet men put hym ye feautees ſeruyce scotlonde ne fraūchyſes dyſheryted hym euermore neuertheles grete lordes englōde agaynſt confyrme ye pea trewſe aboue ſayd ſaue onely quene iſabell yt kynges moder edwarde byſſhop ely lorde montmer reaſon lawe wolde yt fynall pea ſholde made bytwene without comyn aſſent englonde ¶ debate yt bytwene quene iſabell ſyr henry erle lācaſtre leyceſtre rydynge bedford whan ye foreſayd dauid ſpouſed dame ione toure towne barwik ſayd scottes deſpyte englyſſhmen called dame ione ye coūteſſe make pea cowardly pea ordeyned kynges perſone bare al wyte blame wronge makynge accorde done quene roger • rtymer longe ye quene iſabell ne toke handes lordſhyp pountfret almooſt ye londes ony value apperteyned crowne englonde yt kynge dyſpende vſes excheker quene iſabell mortimer gre • e meyny theyr retynue folowed euermore kynges courte went toke ye kynges pryces peny worthes good chepe wherfore coūtre yt came full ſore adrad almooſt deſtroyed thā began ye cominalte englonde haue enuy iſabell quene ſo moche loued whan ſhe came agayne fro fraūce purſue fals traytours ye spenſers ſame tyme ye falſe traytour robert holand • rayed lord ſyr thomas lancaſtre delyuered pryſon wonder preuy ye quene iſabell alſo roger mortimer auayled hȳ lytell taken myghelmaſſe next folowyng rode toward quene iſabell london ſyr thomas wyther ſmote heed beſydes towne ſaynt albons ſyr thomas dwelled ſyr henry erle lancaſtre put hym aſyde drede quene ſhe loued hym wonder moche prayed vnto ye kyng hym yt ſame thomas myght exiled englonde ye noble erle ſyr henry lancaſtre oftentymes herde comyn damour ye englyſſhmen yt diſeaſe done englonde alſo dyuers wronges yt done ye comyn people whiche kyng bare blame wt wronge yonge tender age thought good man awaye ſlake ſclaundre ye kynges perſon yf myght ony maner wyſe ſo ye kyng therof nothynge gylty wherfore peryll lyfe ſo aſſembled retenaunces went ſpake wt ye kynges honour alſo amende eſtate ſyr thomas brotherton erle marſhall ſyr edmond wodſtok yt kynges vncles alſo men londō made theyr othe maynteyn hym ſame quarell theyr cauſe kyng ſholde holde hous meyny king ought haue ryalte ye quene iſabell ſhold deliuer handes ye kynges handes maner lordſhyppes rente townes caſtels yt apperteyned vnto ye crowne englōde quenes dyd meddle none thynge alſo ſyr roger mortimer ſhold abyde dwell vpon owne londes ye whiche londes holpen diſheryte moche people ſo moche ye comyn people deſtroyed wrongfull takynge alſo enquyre whome kynge betrayed falſly deceiued stan hope whoſe coūſeyle scottes went away nyght kynge alſo whoſe coūſeyle ye ordynaunce made kynges crownacyon put downe ſaye kynge amendement helpyng realme honour hym ſholde gouerned ruled xij greteſt kynges frendes muſt herborowed caſtel mortimer went toke theyr herborowe dyuers place ye towne notyngham tho ſore adrad leſt mortimer ſhold deſtroye haſte came vnto kyng edward ſyr willyam moūtagu yt ye caſtell pryuely tolde hym none company ſholde take mortimer without counſeyle helpe wyllyam eland conſtable ſame caſtell truly ſayd ye king loue well therfore counſeyle ye go foreſayd conſtable cōmaunde hym name frende helpe take mortimer thynge left vpon peryll lyfe lymme ſayd moūtagu ſyr lord graūt mercy went forth foreſayd moūtagu came conſtable caſtell told hym kynges wyll anſwered ſayd kynges wyll ſhold done moche myght wolde ſpare maner deth ſo ſwore made othe ſayd ſyr willyam mountagu conſtable herynge helpyng vnto ſame quarell certes dere frende v behoueth werke aduyſe take mortymer ſyth ye keper caſtell haue key warde syr ſayd conſtable ye ſhall vnderſtande ye gate caſtell ben locked locke dame iſabell ſente hyther nyght ſhe hath key therof layeth vnder leueſell bedde tyll morowe ſo ye may come caſtell gate maner wyſe knowe aley ſtretcheth warde vnder ye erth ye foreſayd caſtel yt goth ye weſt whiche aley dame iſabell quene ne none men mortymer ne none cōpany knoweth ſo ſhall lede ye aley ſo ye ſhall come caſtel wtout eſpyenge ony men yt enemyes ſame nyght ſyr william moūtagu lordes quarell ſame conſtable alſo wente hors made ſemblaūt go mortimer ſyght anone mortimer herde theſe tydynges wende yt wold haue gone ouer ſee fere hym anone company toke coū ſeyle amonge lette theyr paſſage ſent lettres anone porte ſo none grete lordes ſholde go home theyr coūtrees yf areſted taken amōge thynges willyam eland conſtable ye foreſayd caſtell priuely lad ſyr william moūtagu company foreſayd waye vnder erth tyl came caſtel went vp toure mortymer ſyr hugh trompyngton theym eſcryed hydouſly ſayd traytours nought ye comē caſtell ye ſhall dye yet euyl deth euerychone anone one yt mountagues cōpany mace ſmote ſame hugh vpon ye heed yt brayn braſt fell ye groūde ſo dyed euyll dethe toke mortymer armed hym ye toures dore whan herde ye noyſe drede whan quene iſabell ſawe ye mortymer taken ſhe made moche ſotowe hert theſe wordes ſayd fayr ſyrs pray yt ye harme body worthy knyght welbeloued frende dere coſyn thā went then came brought mortimer preſented hym vnto kynge edward cōmaunded brynge hym ſafe warde anone conſentyng vnto mortimer doynge herde tell yt taken went hydde p •• urly nyght wente towne eueryche countree heuy herte mournyng chere lyued vpon theyr londes well myght ſo ſame yere yt mortymer taken retynue ix ſcore knyghtes without ſquyers ſergeauntes armes fote men mortymer ladde london ſyr symond bedford ladde hym taken conſtable toure kepe afterwarde mortymers lyf examyned weſtmynſter kynge grete lordes englonde peryll myght fall realme enquyre alſo whiche conſentynge ſyr edwardes deth kynges fader alſo whome scottes eſcaped fro scanhope scotlonde without wyll kyng edward alſo yt charter ragman delyuered vnto scottes wherin homage frautees ye lordes scotlonde conteyned scottes ſholde euer vnto englyſſhe kynge realme scotlōde wherfore abſence dampned draw •• hanged treaſon myſchefe came hym ſaynt andrewes euen yere ye incarnacyon lorde ieſu chryſt ccc rxx ¶ kyng edward gate agayn vnto hym gracyouſly ye homage f • au •• e scotlonde wherof put falſe coūſeyle quene iſabell moder ſyr roger mortymer newly made erle march • haue ye herd ſyr iohn bayloll tyme pea choſen kyng scotlonde bycauſe came ye eldeſt doughter erle dauid huntyngton yt kyng alyſaunders broder scotlond yt dyed without heyre body begoten iohn made feaute homage kyng edward henryes ſone ye thyrde londes scotlonde afterwarde wtſayd homage coūſeyle scottes yere lorde cc lxxiiij ſent vnto pope fals ſuggeſtion made othe vnto foreſayd kyng edward ouer eſtate wyl whiche othe ye pope hym aſſoyled bulles hȳ ſent anone kyng edward wyſt therof ordeyned anone baron came barwyk conquered towne whiche conqueſt ſlayne xxv vij c bayloll yt kyng scotlonde came yelded hym good kynge edward kyng afterward delyuered ye toure london ye grete lordes wt hym tho taken barwyk gaue ſaufconduyte go scotlonde scottes • ith theyr falſnes warred vpon good kyng edward whan ſyr iohn bayloll kyng scotlonde ſawe went ouer ſee vnto dunpier lyued vpon londes wel myght tyll yt scottes wold amēde theyr myſoedes treſpace • ad wt hȳ ſyr edward ſone wherfore ye scottes deſpyte hym called hym ſyr iohn turnlabaerd bycauſe wolde offende ne treſpace agaynſt ye good kyng edward englonde ſo forſoke realme scotlonde ſet therof lytel pryce ſyr iohan dwelled longe tyme fraūce tyll yt dyed ſyr edward ſone receyued herytage dyd homage ye kyng fraūce londes dunpier ſo befell afterward edward yt iohn baylols ſone wt hym ſquyer englōde borne yorkſhyre yt called iohn barnaby edwarde bayloll loued hym moche nygh hym full preuy ſo iohn barnaby debate frenſſhe man ye towne dūpier ſo ſlewe hym went waye ye haſte yt myght ye caſtell haue helpe lord anone came ye officer ye towne take iohn barnaby felon ſyr edward lord holpe hym reſcowed hym night made go ye caſtell ſo went waye came englonde wtout ony harme whan ye kyng fraūce ſawe yt ſyr edward reſcowed felon became wonder wrothe agaynſt ſyr edward anone let areſt hym toke hādes londes dwelled ſyr edward pryſon vnto ye tyme yt ſyr henry beaumont came fraūce whiche henry ſomtyme erle angos scotlonde wyfe put therof whā ye accordemēt bytwene englonde scotlond quene iſabell roger mortimer theyr cōpany ye maryage yt ſhe made bytwene dauyd yt robert ye brus ſone dame ione ye toure kyng edwardes ſyſter englōde well vnderſtode yt ye ende ſhold come ryght yf ſyr edwarde bayloll yt ryght heyre ye realme scotlonde kyng fraunce lowys loued moche ſyr henry hym ful preuy thought make delyueraūce ſyr edwarde bayloll yf myght ony maner wyſe tho prayed ye kyng ye wolde pleaſe noble grace graūt hym ſyr edward baylols body vnto ye next parlyament myght lyue wt tentes meane tyme yt myght ſtande iudged wt peres ye parlyament ye kyng graūted hym prayer made foreſayd edward delyuered pryſon maner aboue ſaid anone priſon ſyr henry toke hym forth wt hym ladde hym englōde made hym dwell pryuely ye maner sandhall vpon ouſe yorkeſhyre lady veſcy ſo ordeyned huge retynue englyſſhemen alſo alyens conquere agayne herytage ſo gaue moche ſiluer ſowdyours alyens helpe hym behyght helpe hym yt myght fayled hym mooſt nede yt tyme donald erle moryf herde tell yt ſyr edwarde baylol priuely come englōde came hym made grete ioye comynge agayn ſayd hym behyght hym yt ye grete lordes scotlonde ſhold hym attendaūt ſhold holde hym kynge ryght heyre scotlōde dyd hȳ homage feaute came ſyr henry beaumont kynge edwarde englonde prayed hym ye waye charite wolde graūt grace ſyr edward bayloll myght ſafely go londe frō sandhal vnto scotlōde cōquere ryght herytaunce scotlonde kynge anſwered ſayd yf ſuffre bayloll go londe scotlonde people wold ſaye yt ſhold aſſentyng vnto ye company ſyr praye ye wolde gyue hym leue take wt hym ſowdyours englyſſhe mē yt myght ſafely lede hȳ londe scotlōde ſyr vpon couenaunt yt yf ſo befall god forbydde dyſcomfyted batayle scottes alſo ye lordes holde wt bayloll ben euer rente haue englonde ye kyng vpon couenaunt graunted theyr bone touchynge hym thoſe yt ſame quarell whiche claymed haue londes rente ye realme scotlōde theſe ye name thoſe lordes purſued foreſayd quarell yt ſaye ſyr edward bayloll whiche chalenged realme scotlonde ſyr henry beaumōt erle angos ſyr dauid stroboly erle atheles ſyr hardy yt may myghtely take scottes night boldly warre vpon let v purſue nyght yf v trauayled ſe hardynes ſcottes ſe ſo trauayled wery ſorer wyll adrad wt v fyght fyerſly ſhall fyght purſue ſo yt y• trauayle ſorowe certes ſemeth v werketh grace wonder gracyous quarell certes ſhal deed may come hȳ v yelde ſyth fader ſet v pryce amonge thynges bayloll people paſſed water erne ſo ſyr roger swynerton ſone fyers angry went forth ſawe people armes full well arayed forth went vnto faught ſlewe toke many wolde abyde neuertheles yt aſſaut wende ben grete hooſt scotlonde whan came morowe gadred togyder reſted whyle whyle ye engliſſhmen reſted noble baron thomas veſcy noble baron ſtafford pricked theyr horſes vp ye hylles kepe eſtres y• coūtree prycked vp ſawe grete hooſt good araye ordeyned theyr wynges helmes ſheldes ſhynynge comynge vpon came tho two lordes agayn baylols folke ſayd loue god good cōforte ye ſhall haue batayle anone right tho ſpake ſyr fouke ye ſone gareyne baron grete renome dedes armes syrs vnderſtāde wyll ſaye haue ſeen many dyuers wynges wel amonge ſaraſyns iewes amonge y• ſcottes yet ſawe neuer fourth parte wynge fyght therfore yf ye wyll abyde enemyes ynough fight againſt yf good hert good courage loſt therfore loue god let v take v good herte let v bolde thynke neuer wyues ne childrē onely cōquere enemyes batayle helpe lorde god ſhall ouercome yt came hooſt scottes towarde full ſurely agaynſt ſyr edward bayloll thre bataylles well arayed armure wonder fyerſly came towarde baylols company whā ſyr donald erle marcil y• scottes ſawe ſaid robert brus ſone robert brus theſe wordes syr roberte ſayd full ſore forthynketh herte yt theſe people bayloll hathe brought wt hym ſholde dye dynt ſcottes ſwerdes lyth yt chryſten men therfore thȳketh yt grete charite ſende vnto yelde mercy raunſom greuous raunſom moche haue takē londe done yll certes ſayd ſyr robert y• brus haue wel perceyued yu art enemy traytour scotlonde ſyth yu wylt conſent ſaue deedly enemyes yt haue done v ſo moche ſorowe ſhame ſemeth well ye theyr aſſent certes roberte ſayd ſyr donald falſly ye lye theyr company ne theyr cōſent haſtely ye ſhall ſe wyll fyght wt rather ony cōpany certes ſyr roberte ſayd ſhal maugre thy heed aſſayle thou prycked theyr ſtedes fyerſly gaſkmo theyr wynges folowed rēge tho came mette wt bayloll cōpany hangynge bough ſtrayte paſſage ſo faſt haſted vnto englyſſhmen thouſandes fell groūde eche ouer hepe bothe hors mā syr bayloll men myghtely ſtode agaynſt faſt ſlewe scottes groūde many fore woūded ſo longe tyll ſtode vpon foyned wt theyr ſwerdes ſperes theyr bodyes full ſore trauayled vpon tyll yt became wōders wery wyſt y• scottes lefte alyue fledde away ſaue themſelfe beſt maner myght tho purſued ſyr edwarde ba towne pauylyons dy ched ſo drede scottes made many aſſautes wt gonne engynes towne wherwt deſtroyed many fayre houſes chirches alſo beten downe y• erth grete ſtones ſpytefully came gonne engynes neuertheles y• scottes kept well towne ye two kynges myght come therin longe tyme kynges abode ſo lōge tyll thoſe wtin town fayled vitayles alſo ſo wery wakynge yt wyſt ye ſhall vnderſtand yt scottes gladly y• day houre batayle yt philip aſſygned whan ye kynge fraūce herde yt nexte nyght ſet tentes fyre remeued wente awaye cowardly yt ye towne ye caſtel beſyeged ſeynge al none helpe ne ſocour king fraūce ne men alſo yt theyr vitayles wtin ſpended waſted faute vitayles freſſhing ete horſes hoūdes cattes myce kepe theyr treuth longe myght whā ſawe foūde amonge ye laſt yt thynge amōge dyuers place naked borne ſaue onely theyr ſhertes preuy clothes helde theyr ſwerdes naked poynt downward theyr hādes put rope halter aboute theyr neckes yelded vp key ye towne caſtell kyng edward ſate iudgement rode hym vnto place done dethe ſo ſe ye execucyon done dome kynges cōmaundement wente fote men armes archer grete multytude cheſtre ſhyre men ſtrengthynge ye lordes yt brought erle dethe drede leeſt ye erle ſholde reſcowed taken whan came london thus paſſed forth cite vnto deth toke full pacyently whoſe ſoule god haue mercy amen came auſtyn freres toke vp ye body heed good erle wepen redy theyr batayle redy ye place fyght vtteraūce ye kyng ceſſe toke quarell handes forth ryght preſent exiled duke herford terme x yere duke norfolke euermore ſyr thomas arundell archebiſſhop caū terbury exiled yt ſame tyme euer depoſed ſee malyce kyng anone theſe thre worthy lordes cōmaunded defended ye kynges realme anone gate ſhyppes dyuers hauens went ouer ſee dyuers lōdes eche waye ye duke norfolke went veniſe died whoſe ſoule god haue mercy amen kynge rychard made clerke ſyr roger walden arche byſſhop caūterbury ¶ xxij yere kynge richardes regne fals coūſeyle ymaginacyon couetous men aboute hym made ordeyned blancke chartres made enſealed al maner ry men throughout ye realme ſo moche yt compelled diuers people ſet theyr ſeales therto done grete couetyſe wherfore al good hertes ye realme clene turned away fro ye kyng euer vtter deſtruccyon ende hym yt ſo hygh ſo excellent prynce kyng couetous fals coūſeyle falſely betrayed ala pyte ye ſuche kynge myght ſe kynge rychard ſet kyngdome ryall londe englonde ferme vnto foure perſones whiche theſe ſyr wyllyā scrope erle wylſhyre treſourer englond ſyr iohn buſſhe henry grene ſyr iohn bagot knyghtes whiche turned myſchefe deth within lytell tyme ye ſhall fynde afterwarde wryten ¶ kyng rychard de grete ordynaūce went hymſelf ouer ſee irlonde many grete lordes wt hym grete hooſtes ſtrength theyr kynge wt men armes archer moche grete ſtuffe ryght good ordynaūce longed vnto warre paſſed ouer ye ſee ordeyned made 〈◊〉 edmond langley vncle ye duke yorke lewtenaū • englonde abſence gouernaūce coūſey • e wi •• hym came erle arundel ſo •• heyre whiche kepynge ſyr iohn ſhelley knight ſomtyme wt • erle huntyngdon wt duke exceſtre whiche tho caſtell 〈◊〉 gate suſſex ſtale awaye came calays well worthely kepte tyll theſe two lordes comē calays thā worthy duke archebyſſhop caū terbury arundell ſhypped ye hauen calais drewe theyr courſe northward arryued yorkſhyre rauenſporne faſt wydelyngton came entred fyrſt londe two lordes hym theyr meyny moche people realme herde comynge knewe yt anone drewe vnto hym welcomed theſe lordes ſo couraged maner thynge paſſed forth londe gadred moche people whan kyng rychard herde wyſt theſe two lordes comen agayne englonde londed kynge lefte ordynaūce irlonde came englondward haſte myght came caſtell • lyut abode take counſeyle myght done hym came none whā ſyr thomas percy erle worceſtre yt ye kynges ſteward wyſt knewe anone came hall amonge ye people brake yerde ye ryall kynges houſholde anone euery man diſperpied went waye forſoke theyr mayſter ſouerayn lorde lefte hym alone thus kynge rycharde brought downe deſtroyed ſtode hym ſelfe alone without comforte ſocour ony good counſeyle ony man ala pite ryall kyng anone came tydȳges ſyr henry boling broke vp ſtronge power people ye ſquyers englonde reyſed vp ſhyres ſtrengthyng hym agaynſt kyng rychard thus ſoone comen north coūtree bryſtowe mette ſyr wyllyam scrope erle wylſhyre treſourer englonde ſyr iohn buſſhe ſyr henry grene iohn bagot eſcaped frō went ouer ſee irlonde theſe thre knyghtes taken theyr herdes ſmytten thus died theyr fals couetyſe kynge rychard taken brought vnto duke anone ye duke put hȳ faſt warde ſtronge holde vnto comynge london rumour london ſtronge noyſe kynge rychard came weſtmynſter people london ranne thyder wolde haue done moche harme hurte theyr woodnes ye mayre alderman worthy men ceſſed fayre wordes turned home agayne london ¶ ſyr iohn slake dene kynges chapell weſtmynſter taken brought london put pryſon ludgate iohn bagot taken irlonde people englonde londes ſayd yt lyue many yere deth whether alyue deed people helde theyr fals opinyon byleue many moche people came grete myſchefe foule dethe ye ſhal afterward whan kyng henry wyſt knewe yt deed let • ere hym beſt maner cloſed fayre cheſt wt dyuers ſpyceryes ba • • e cloſed hym lynnen cloth ſaue viſage left open men myght ſe perſone men ſo brought london torche light brennynge ſaint paules chirche maſſe dirige wt moche reuerēce ſolempnite ſeruyce whā done brought ſaynt paules abbey weſtmynſter al hole ſeruyce agayn weſtmȳſter brought langley buryed whoſe ſoule god haue mercy amen ¶ ye fyrſt yere kynge henryes regue helde chryſtmaſſe ye caſtell wyndſore xij euen came duke awemarle vnto kynge colde hym duke surrey duke exceſtre erle saliſbury ye erle gloceſtre moo theyr affynite accorded make mommynge vnto ye kynge xij daye nyght purpoſed ſlee ye kyng reuelyng thus ye duke awemarle warned ye kyng kyng came london pryuely haſte yt myght gete hym helpe ſocour cōforte coūſeyle anone theſe yt wolde haue put ye kynge deth fledde haſte yt myght knewe well theyr coūſeyle bewrayed fledde ye duke surrey erle salyſbury wt theyr meyny vnto ye towne chicheſtre people towne wold haue areſted tolde ſtande theyr areſtyng ſtode defence fought manly ye laſt ouercomen takē ſmote duke heed surrey erles heed salyſbury many moo put theyr quarter ſackes theyr heedes grey ri • hen pryſoner kepte hym faſt holde tyll raūſomed pryſoners marche kepte hym longe tyme holde laſt made hȳ wedde one doughters kepte hym ſtyll wyfe ſoone dyed kyng henry knowynge miſchefe victory brought ye carackes cambre wyn chelſee • anted theſe goodes one theſe carackes ſodeynly brent lordes theyr people turned home agayne went ferther y• tyme ¶ ye ſame tyme serle yeman kynge agayne englonde ſafete thanked god ¶ viij yere kyng henryes regne man yt called walſſhe clerke appeled knight yt called ſir percyuall snowdon treaſon ioyned fight ye vtteraūce within lyſtes daye place tyme aſſigned lymyted done ended smythfelde whiche daye thoſe two perſones came ye felde fought ſore myghtely togyder laſt knyght ouercame clerke made hȳ yelde hym creaūt fals empechement yt ſayd hym deſpoiled armure drawen felde tyburne hanged knyght takē grace good man ¶ ſame yere ſyr henry erle northumberlōde lorde bardolf came scotlonde preiudyce deſtruceyon kynge henry wherfore northcoūtre aroſe vpon fought wt diſcōfited toke ſmo • e hedes quartred theyr bodyes ſent heed erle quarter ye lorde bardolf londō ſet vpon loudō brydge fals treaſon purpoſed agaynſt ye kyng ¶ ix yere kyng henryes regne ſyr edmond holland erle kent made amyrall englonde kepe ye ſee went ſee wt many ryal ſhyppes ful well arayed apparayled enarmed many good man armes archer good defence warre kynges name englonde ſo londed laſt coſte brytayn yle briak al folke beſyeged caſtell aſſauted withſtode hym grete defence ſtrength anone layd ordynaunce layenge gonne came quarell ſmote good erle edmond heed caught deth woūde yet left tyll goten caſtell therin good lord dyed vpon whoſe ſoule god haue mercy amen meyny came home agayne englonde wt erles body buryed amonge aūceſtres right worthely ¶ ſame yere grete froſt englōde • ured xv wekes ¶ x yere kyng henryes regne fourth came se • eſſhall henaud meyny englonde ſeke auentures gete worſhyp dedes armes bothe horſbacke fote maner poyntes warre ye seneſſhall chalenged ye erle somerſet erle delyue red hȳ full manfully al chalenges put aduerſary worſt al poyntes wan grete worſhip ye degre ye felde ye nexte day came ye felde man armes seneſſhals party agaynſt came ſyr rychard arundel knyght henaud ye better hym fote one poynt brought hym knee thyrde daye came man armes ye felde agaynſt hym came ſyr iohn corne wayle knyght manly knyghtly quytte hȳ maner poyntes agaynſt aduerſary ye better ye felde fourth daye came man armes henaud felde agaynſt came ſyr iohn chaynes ſone manly quytte hym agaynſt aduerſary caſt hors man ye felde kynge manhode tyme dubbed hym knyght fyfth daye came man armes henaudes party ye felde hym came ſyr iohn ſtewarde knight manfully quytte maner poyntes better ye ſyxth daye came henaud hym came willyam porter ſquyer manfully quytte hym better ye felde kynge dubbed hym knyght ye ſame tyme ſeuenth daye came man armes henaud felde came iohn standiſſhe ſquyer manfully quytte hym aduerſary better hym felde ye kynge dubbed hym knyght ſame daye ye ſame day came man armes henaud hym came ſquyer gaſcoyne proudly māly quytte hym aduerſary better hym anone kynge dubbed hym knyght viij day came felde two men armes henaud came two ſowdyours calays whiche bretherne yt called burghes well manly quytte theyr aduerſaryes better ye felde thus ended ye chalenges many grete worſhyppes kynge reuerence theſe worthy ſtrafigers made grete feeſt gaue many riche gyftes thā toke theyr leue went home agayne theyr owne countree ¶ x • yere kynge henryes regne fourth grete batayle done ſmyth felde bytwene two ſquyers one called gloceſtre appellaunt arthur defendaūt well manly fought togyder longe tyme kynge theyr manfulnes grace toke theyr quarell handes made go felde one ſo deuyded theyr batayle kyng gaue grace ¶ xij yere kyng henryes regne fourth • yſdie ſquyer wale rebell ryſer ſupporter owen glendre whiche dyd moche deſtruccyon people wale taken brought london came iuſtyees dampned treaſon layde hurdell ſo drawen tyburne cite hanged let downe agayne heed ſmytten body quartred ſent foure townes heed ſet vpon london brydge ¶ xiij yere kynge henryes regne tho dyed ſyr iohn beauford ye erle somerſet capytayne calays buryed abbey toure hyll whoſe ſoule god haue mercy amen ¶ ſame yere lorde thomas kyng henryes ſone wedded ye coū teſſe somerſet ¶ ſame yere came embaſſadours fraunce englonde fro duke burgoyn vnto prynce englonde kyng henryes ſone heyre haue helpe ſocour mē armes archer againſt duke orlyaunce went ouer ſee erle arundel ſyr gylbert vmfreuyll erle kent lorde cobham ſyr iohn oldcaſtell many good knyghtes worthy ſquyers men armes good archer fraūce came parys ye duke burgoyn receyued welcomed theſe englyſſhe lordes meyny done hȳ wyte yt duke orlyaūce comen ſaynt clowe faſt parys wt grete nombre men armes arbalaſtres thyder went englyſſhmen fought gate y• brydge ſaynt clowe ſlewe many frenſſhmen arbalaſtres remenaūt fledde wold longer abyde thā englyſſhmen came agayn parys toke theyr leue ye duke came ſafe agayne englonde duke gaue grete gyftes anone ye duke orlyaūce ſent embaſſadours englonde kyng henry iiij beſechinge helpe ſocour agaynſt deedly enemy ye duke burgoyne kynge made thomas ſone duke clarence ſone iohn duke bedforde ſone vmfrey duke gloceſtre ſyr thomas beauford erle dorſet duke awemarle made duke yorke ye kyng ordeyned ſone ſyr thomas duke clarēce ſir thomas beauford erle dorſet ſyr iohn cornwyll many lordes knyghtes ſquyers men armes archer go ouet ſee fraūce helpynge ſtrengthynge duke orlyaunce theſe worthy lordes wt theyr retynue ſhypped hamton ſayled ouer y• ſee normādy londed hogges mette wt y• lorde hambe theyr londynge vij men armes frenſſhmen thre ſergeaūtes armes put flyght takē vij c men armes iiij c horſes without thoſe ſlayne felde ſo rode forth fraūce toke caſtles townes ſlewe many frenſſhemen withſtode toke many pryſoners rode ſo paſſed forth tyll came burdeux reſted whyle ſet countree pea reſted tyll vyntage redy ſayle ye duke meyny came home englond ſafete thāked god ¶ ſame yere kynges coyne chaunged throughout englonde kynge coūſeyle ſaye noble halfe noble ferthynge golde ¶ xiiij yere kyng hērpes regne fourth let make galays warre hoped haue paſſed grete ſee ſo forth ieruſalem haue ended lyfe god vyſyted hym ſoone wt infirmite grete ſekenes myght well endure whyle ſo ſeruently taken brought bed weſtmȳſter fayre chambre lay bed aſked chamberlayne called ye chambre yt lay anſwered ſayd ieruſalem ſayd yt prophecy ſayd yt ſhold make ende dye ieruſalē made hym redy vnto god dyſpoſed wyll ſoone died caried water frō weſtmynſter barge vnto feuerſham frō then caryed caūterbury londe wt moche torche lyght brennynge ye abbey chryſtchirche entered buryed beſyde ſaint thomas caūterburyes ſhryne thus ended ye worthy kyng henry mydlent ſondaye ye yere lorde cccc xiij vpon whoſe ſoule god haue mercy amen martyn y• v pope iohn xiiij yere mā choſen concyle conſtance depoſed y• ſtroue ſo came pea chirche whiche longe tyme afore deſyred neceſſary y• defence fayth y• myghtyeſt pope euer ryches grete iudge edifyed townes walles ſtretes deſtroyed hereſyes brent ¶ ye ſeconde yere kynge henryes regne held coūſeyle ye lordes ye realme weſtmȳſter put hym demaūde prayed beſouhgt theyr goodnes theyr good coūſeyle good wyll ſhewe hym touchyng ye tytell right yt normandy gaſcoyn guyen whiche ye king fraūce whelde wrongfully vnryghtfully y• whiche aunceſtres hȳ true tytell cōqueſt right herytage whiche normādy gaſcoyn guyen ye good kyng edward wyndſore aunceſtres hym holden theyr lyf tyme lordes gaue hym coūſeyle ſende embaſſadours kyng fraūce coūſeyle yt ſhold gyue vp vnto hym ryght herytage yt ſaye normandy gaſcoyn guyen y• whiche predeceſſours holden afore hȳ el wold wynne ſtrengthe ſwerde ſhorte tyme ye helpe almighty god dolphyn fraūce anſwered embaſſadours ſaydi maner kyng ouer yonge tender age make ony warre agaynſt hȳ lyke yet good warryour make ſuche cōqueſt vpon hym ſomwhat ſcorne deſpyte ſent hȳ tonne full tenes balles bycauſe ſhold haue ſomwhat playe withall lordes wolde become hym better mayntayn ony warre anone lordes yt embaſſadours toke theyr leue came englonde agayne tolde kynge couſeyle vngoodly anſwere yt dolphin preſent y• whiche ſente kynge whan kynge herde theyr wordes y• anſwere y• dolphyn wonder ſore agreued ryght euyll apayed towarde frenſſhmen towarde kynge dolphyn thought auēge hym ſoone god wold ſende hym grace myght anone let make tenes balles dolphyn y• haſte myght grete gonſtones dolphyn playe withall anone kynge ſent lordes helde grete coūſeyle weſtmynſter told anſwer yt dolphin worthy preſent yt ſent hym lordes playe wtall ye kyng lordes accorded ſhold redy armes wt theyr power beſt araye yt myght done gete men armes archer myght goten ſtuffe yt longed warre redy wt theyr retynue mete southhampton lāmaſſe nexte folowynge without ony delaye wherfore ye kynge ordeyned nauy ſhyppes maner ſtuffe vytayle lōged ſuche warryour maner ordynaunce hauen southhampton ye nombre ccc xx ſayles thā fell grete dyſeaſe foule myſchefe thre lordes whiche kyng truſted moche falſe couetyſe purpoſed ymagined kynges deth thought haue ſlayne hym bretherne taken ſee whiche thre lordes named thus ſyr rycharde erle cambrydge broder ye duke yorke ye ſeconde lord scrope treſourer englōde y• thyrd ſir thomas gray knyght north coūtree theſe thre lordes aforeſayd lucre money made promeſſe vnto y• frenſſhmen haue ſlayne kyng henry fyfth bretherne falſe trayne ſodeynly ben ware almyghty god grete grace helde holy hande ouer ſaued theſe perillous meiny haue done receyued y• frenſſhmen millyon gold openly proued theyr fals treaſon thre iudged deth y• iudgement ſholde ladde hampton without northgate heded thus ended theyr lyues theyr fals couetyſe treaſon anone done kynge meyny made redy went ſhyppe ſayled forth xv hondred ſhyppes arryued within seyne kydecauſe prynces ye londe called coūſeyle ſet aparte onely ſo ſayd realme thoſe ſaid lordes ſholde deſtroyed vtterly opēly ſhewed bloreheth wolde haue ſlayne ye erle salyſbury ſaluacyon theyr lyues alſo ye ye warre moche truſted whā thus aſſembled made theyr felde kyng ſent cōmyſſyons preuy ſeales vnto ye lordes realme come wayte hym theyr mooſt beſt defenſable aray ſo euery man came ſuche wiſe yt kyng ſtronger people ye duke yorke ye erles warwyk salyſbury noted euery lorde englonde durſt diſobey ye quene ſhe ruled peaſybly yt done ye kyng whiche good well diſpoſed man thā whan ye kyng comen place duke yorke felaw ſhyp made theyr felde ye ſtrōgeſt wyſe purpoſed verily haue bydē fought ye nyght andrewe trollop ye olde ſowdyours calays wt grete felawſhyp ſodeynly departed ye duke hooſt wente ſtreyght ye kynges feld ioyouſly receyued knewe ye entent ye lordes alſo ye maner theyr felde ye duke yorke wt lordes ſeynge deceyued toke coūſeyle ſhortly ſame nyght departed ye felde leuynge behynde mooſt party theyr people kepe ye felde tyll morowe duke yorke wt ſecond ſone departed wale toward irlonde leuynge eldeſt ſone yt erle marche wt erles warwik salyſbury whiche rode togyder wt thre foure perſones ſtreyght deuenſhyre helpe ayde one denham ſquyer gate thē ſhyppe coſt xj ſcore noble wt ſame ſhyppe ſayled frō then ī garneſey refreſſhed fro then ſayled calais receyued ye caſtell yt poſterne ye towne wyſt duke yorke toke ſhyppynge wale ſayled ouer irlonde well receyued ¶ ye erles marche warwyk salyſbury entred calays erle warwyk went irlonde kynge henry beynge wt hooſt ye felde knowynge ſodeyn departynge morowe foūde none ye felde ye ſaid lordes ſent ye haſte men folowe purſue take met god wolde kyng went ludlowe deſpoyled caſtell towne ſent ducheſſe yorke child ye ducheſſe bokyngham ſyſter ſhe kepte longe tyme forth wt kyng ordeyned duke somerſet capytayn calays theſe lordes ſo departed afore ſayd proclaymed rebelles grete traytours ye duke somerſet toke hym ye ſowdyours yt departed ye felde made hym redy haſte go calays take poſſeſſyon offyce whan came foūde ye erle warwik therin capitayn ye erles marche salyſbury alſo londed scale went guynes receyued fortuned ſome tho ſhyppes came ouer hȳ came calays hauen theyr free wyll ye ſhypmen ought fauour ye erle warwik duke somerſet whiche ſhyppes taken dyuers men ienyn finkhyl iohn felow kaylles purſer whiche byheded ſoone calays ¶ came men dayly ouer ſee theſe lordes calays began wexe ſtronger ſtronger borowed moche good ſtaple yt ſyde ye duke somerſet beynge guynes gate people hym whiche came ſcarmyſſhed wt calays calays whiche endured many dayes duryng ſcarmyſſhynge moche people came ouer dayly vnto theſe lordes tyme ye aduyſe counſeyle ye lordes calays ſente ouer mayſter denham grete warwyk ye aduyſe lordes toke al ſhyppes māned well ſayled hȳſelfe irlonde ſpeke wt duke yorke take aduiſe ſhold entre englonde whan ben done crandes returned agayn toward calays brought wt hym moder ye coūteſſe saliſbury comynge ye weſt countre vpon ſee duke exceſtre admyral englōde beynge ye grace dieu accōpanyed wt many ſhippes warre mette wt erle warwyk flete fought ye ſubſtaūce ye people neuertheles two dartes ſperes brode ſparthes fyght wt one hande theſe men forſake tyllynge londe kepe paſture beeſtes vſe longe berdes longe locke hangynge downe behynde theyr hedes vſe crafte flaxe woll metall marchaūdyſe gyue ydlenes ſlouth reken reſt lykynge fredome rycheſſe though scotlonde doughter irlonde vſe harpe tymbre tabour neuertheles iryſſhe men connynge two maner inſtrumentes muſyke harpe tymbre yt armed wt wyre ſtrenges braſſe whiche inſtrumentes though playe haſtely ſwyftly make ryght mery armony melody thycke tewnes werbles note begyn bemoll playe ſecretly vnder dyme ſowne grete ſtrenges turne agayne vnto ſame ſo greteſt party crafte hydeth craft wolde ſeme though crafte ſo hydde ſholde aſhamed yf take theſe men ben euyll maners theyr lyuynge paye tythynges wedde lawfully ſpare theyr alyes y• broder weddeth broders wyfe ben beſy betraye theyr neyghbours bere ſparthes theyr hādes ſtede ſtaues fyght agaynſt truſt mooſt theſe men ben varyable vnſtedfaſt trechours gylefull deleth nedeth beware gyle crafte pea brēnynge brondes hony gall malyce knyghthode haue ſuche maners yt ſtrōge warre batayle ne true pea become goſſeps yt wyll falſly betraye ye goſſeprede holy kynrede eueryche drynketh others blode whan ſhedde loue ſomdele theyr nouryce theyr playferes whiche ſouke ye ſame mylke yt ſouked whā chyldren purſue theyr bretherne theyr coſyns
